# 如何以“他说他喜欢用长剑的女子，而我只会双刀”为开头，写一个 HE 的故事？
- 点赞数：9268
- 更新时间：2022年03月12日21时05分55秒
- 回答url：https://www.zhihu.com/question/472496087/answer/2079746223
<body>
 <p data-pid="Uk2EIJA0">完结啦完结啦，全文约5.7k字。放一个旧文链接，任何人没有看过我的旧文我都会伤心的好吗QAQ（其实是因为我把两篇文写串了……）</p><a href="https://www.zhihu.com/question/465978427/answer/1970969045" data-draft-node="block" data-draft-type="link-card" class="internal">如何以「我原以为自己是女主……」为开头写一篇小故事？</a>
 <p data-pid="BJ3oG1tX">他说他喜欢用长剑的女子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wV-k5bZe">而我只会双刀。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MlEGdD9v">——</p>
 <h2>1.双刀</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KOdZM5Yl">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5yk4sp_H">你tm玩我呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BTtlsMh8">上次还说喜欢用双刀的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="60l5vjvf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rPFBwbXs">我沉吟半晌，拿起双刀，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bqAZfmXX">左一把右一把驾到南竹的脖子上，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="skwWjfqV">又问了一遍：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fK1v1QR2">“想清楚了吗？喜欢用双刀的还是用长剑的？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mU76iCYM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Xo9aOF1I">南竹：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ROwIkDwQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PKl6jY5f">他说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OEBz5t5z">“其实......双不双刀剑不剑的不打紧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mO54CiZu">重点是，我喜欢女子......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2t9S02n2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XFllW-TZ">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jC5YqBe4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D2xFi5jn">这人真是的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FP6twzOD">我都为你学双刀了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LPmLQtCn">你就不能放宽一下标准？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gqDLSfwX">要求这么苛刻怎么找对象啊？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FPohfEnb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0WpHPObW">舔不动，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OEQ3xSVD">失望。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lZwqHj5-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KnktzYnO">留下瑟瑟发抖的南竹，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y4i4mel2">我提着双刀走了。</p>
 <p data-pid="K6JzVTFQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ez0qjOTO">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YoPgSXKF">生气地扔了双刀。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9IzrbgEm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TrB3st6X">转身走两步，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VBNbymWD">我想了想，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VmxDivlH">又跑回来捡起双刀。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CiULa_zg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QoiX6Jg5">好贵的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rZ-le2gF">——</p>
 <h2>2.长剑山</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jWOjm3TB">第二天，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ilQ5yIfZ">我重整旗鼓，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DSx82JY-">决定最后再舔一次南竹。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B2nTzG-u">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3GaBcsn7">我要学长剑！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cqS_-Z8D">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C0m5l6tc">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pVn1tHPg">去长剑派拜师。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7YCx47P-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NnV8kTi0">过程很顺利，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uI8NP3Pz">我拜了个师，磕了个头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DfbbLqtE">成了长剑派四弟子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xoXcGXrR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wMqC7d_J">我有一个大师兄，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wFIDhebM">总是笑眯眯的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZYFYPWob">像狐狸。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JGm0Ia45">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iGG6wgze">二师姐是个拽姐，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YKoIxylG">爱穿紫色留仙裙。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Z3vK3jrZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mh9CfNWs">三师兄是个光头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z8fIlrnw">头上有六个圆戒疤，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NhBwS7Fk">好像以前是个和尚。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p6NLSTNY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SqZcwJdy">长剑派还不错，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fjCgJh42">师门弟子个个颜值高，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yrDiZgqg">简直是颜狗天堂。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_4poceZq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VMqA8Gxf">就是......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ervt96Q8">这儿的生活条件忒简陋了点。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EofX-1bf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cJw8zWWd">长剑派在长剑山上，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YM3aTx5a">长剑山上有好多山洞，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Zv8aXaJw">我们都住山洞里。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oU0qzdZO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jVpUe8HH">所以，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="piBaB4Ky">外派人都叫我们，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KcDg-XoJ">山顶洞人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bp-OZNi6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oxh4GeXX">对了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yGJGoWJL">我还有个师父。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="az3fNFmQ">他长着一张娃娃脸，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mvB1fWHf">总在睡觉，一般见不着人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uXiFQ9Sy">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jfk58CwV">我刚来时，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pPTipLub">因为总见不到师父，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TSuIqslI">很担心。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xi-L3Hws">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EOhDdz4L">大师兄好像看穿了我的担忧，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4N_RFIMO">笑眯眯地拍了拍我的肩膀，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9zd5DEpz">说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bqX29B6j">“放心，你就当师父死了吧。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VH5q8BGD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AxazaKyO">我有点疑惑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eZzOQnuV">咱师门说话都这么礼貌的吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Op3Lh3F8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LdYY23Lw">我问他：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gECQhrVn">“那谁教我长剑？你吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4xAGBlep">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qDHoUtSd">大师兄摊了摊手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NOSlf60k">“我可不会。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UaoX1OKk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NU6vJJTb">我看向了二师姐。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cA6jKFeX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u28Le8kv">二师姐：拽姐脸.jpg</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s8dYlW-A">“不会。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P5ccrQlg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rJRu9XtR">我再看向三师兄。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G50GLayx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NUMp7JPI">三师兄微微一笑，双手合十。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sznM1pmC">“小僧也不会。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y7u80azV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wSwuKp4w">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K8HUA_Ju">我蒙圈了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bkxFv2qV">“那你们都学了个啥？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ihMhcUvD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rNa-Gcds">大师兄叹了一口气。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="L8CWQScF">二师姐沉默。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Kx59mqAH">三师兄念了一句阿弥陀佛。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_BNFlpWK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="X5Qr9pz9">这三人相互交换眼神，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2urmcdR1">很有默契地转身走了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BlC2fdfW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-ToMKNuE">别走啊！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gineJjMk">我不懂，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MwFVu8j0">你们啥意思啊？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tcv8j-rk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="coscPe-D">这时候，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KG19e1qt">师父睡醒了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O783-hkW">他顶着一团乱糟糟的卷毛，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tpO4gCHV">打着哈欠从洞府里走出来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wHCKD3H6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="E8FW1jQV">他看见我，走过来拍了拍我的头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YGAxEZdj">说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UKEu3XLN">“小四啊，今天是不是轮到你山下去讨饭……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rY_KRTed">啊咳咳咳，是不是轮到你养家糊口了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sZ_SLM6f">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DCF0iReI">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k9Rnz0L6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H2zDmTyl">师父咦了一声，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Bb7iHBVE">摸着下巴说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="58Pa8z_S">“看来他们没跟你说呀。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-NmTwD2K">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OO7WpHDh">“没关系，那为师来。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="X2tOMQGY">师父笑着对我说。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h6q332rP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OtYcmntu">不知道为啥，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6TljPR0r">我从他那张可爱的正太脸上看出了恶魔的笑意。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nwR3gck8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y5GLqgDx">……</p>
 <p data-pid="4wn-9eKT">后来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i1-rqDd0">每每我回想起师父时，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qCikYSSF">总是扼腕叹息，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="apapZHUu">这样的人怎么就没有英年早逝呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FPwQYmhC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YEZI0oHp">那天，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IQzEStCu">我得知了长剑派，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="obs02lhr">是个黑心门派。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Azkz2u-G">我师父，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jgl5_MUD">是个黑心师父。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T6FwTZCb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mmVz1PTZ">简单来说，这个门派，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jTu9qRvw">啥也不教，穷得叮当响，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kBBmfgAO">师父认徒弟，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fKDbyrEU">是为了让徒弟去山下讨饭回来养活他。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KwneOTra">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gsHFCheC">那时，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hQg_-hQ2">我听完师父说的这番话，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LGl2dRz5">当场就给气笑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XhW7__Ct">抽出双刀，架他脖子上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jI4Z7Kel">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GYw1MXnM">我对他说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ouGDn-ZI">“讨饭多麻烦，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ss_gVeGO">我看你以后都不用吃饭了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KR9Piqy2">——</p>
 <h2>3.师父和师兄们</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pcq9i4a4">师父对脖子上的刀视若无睹，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NGqI5jW9">这倒让我有几分敬佩了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o1mnuhu3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="e9OVHawU">他试图萌混过关，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Iz0pxvKI">对我眨巴了一下眼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LSTcMS24">说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s9l95nQ4">“小四，不要这么暴躁。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HYKgB8-R">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7TM6dbLV">呵，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q0EYIzUO">我面无表情地收紧了刀，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pr8P1PCr">刀锋几乎要划破他的脖子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U9DutR7a">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jmwENlRz">“哎哎哎，不要冲动嘛~”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zudH2_V5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MxZhZSm5">突然，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mDBIqpc5">我眼前虚影一晃，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-HArnwCn">耳边划过风声。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xcgLyN5B">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kv6ZNZEU">只一瞬间，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZRBqJbDk">师父已挣脱双刀的束缚，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qL2J_3DF">绕到我身后。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I73bJnEY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gf56JjZG">好快！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bNqkQAYG">我瞪大了双眼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R7U_2OzY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a9IADzCA">他站在我背后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9cgfBLVC">贴得很近，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="logbCcbw">我几乎能感受到他呼出的气息。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mIOrv8Pl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kF9ZDfja">我感觉到，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="frQiDTl8">他伸手摸了摸我的发顶。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_47ABKz2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FQ25E-M2">看不见他的脸，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TupGWfhi">我才发觉他的嗓音冷冽得像山泉，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YCrp-Uut">一点都不正太。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RSEOx3jD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0GVgbKZR">他摆足了高人风范，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gxpbY_is">才缓缓道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HHEGKKax">“你不好奇你的几个师兄为何拜入我门下，至今未离开吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fS-Evys2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wVj0T4rZ">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J8tik4qb">“不好奇。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wQzUmurJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ePZulp9s">师父：……？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HGfRrkcJ">啊这，没法接了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pIoQwSXw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yaqA4LvO">我嘲讽一笑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="94RB8PDd">想钓我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qCLl_XYo">没门。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GakHGNXR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8_5keVDf">我转身走了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UiFZLMZL">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m_-p1rzB">一刻钟后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bi26419N">师父抱着我的腿，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wUY1gK2r">求着我不要走。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IOEFpBUR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LPQ5Sib_">他苦苦哀求：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KRd3q6Rq">“小四，不要走啊~</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gZX1L_pf">你真的不想学我的独门轻功吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JT6Qz3rE">学会之后身轻如燕飞花摘叶踏雪飞鸿快如闪电的那种……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m0ecyQNh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MEItwwJ0">我无情地掰开他的手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ycBvS86D">抽腿就走。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t1GM_K8T">这个傻子我是一秒都不想再见了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_s8aQ52u">我要离开这个虚假宣传的门派。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aUjhJnkO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0xeq7fqv">走远了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="teJRVgqV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MOMHKukH">身后突然传来师父的喊声。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ymLGrIcI">“小四，你别走！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="op_rrFY9">不就是长剑吗？我可以学！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VCQL3Olb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i7mTUDIJ">我下山的脚步一顿，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Lj-PxDjb">头上冒出一个问号：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XHiD_5Ng">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8Sf4UqZT">也许是被这似曾相识的舔狗语录触动了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZEWOYsAf">也许是一时脑子抽筋了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x54ZJGp7">反正最后我答应留一段时间先。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EE3g5dbb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HtL6HVXR">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D6vbVgE5">师父真的去学长剑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WMCRmSpD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Rq0GbD-S">我亲眼看着他去山下的路边摊，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BfuV5Kkp">买了一本小册子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8jHXGjGM">上面歪歪斜斜地写着几个字：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="14HSc1Fb">绝世剑谱。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wB1drhEl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2TtTVUmE">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WWjhLHYb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OLnNtPoE">他去后山削了根竹子做成木剑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y6rj_a3W">对着这个散页的小册子练了七天，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7JwygNEd">然后，成为了长剑高手！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vhmATS0w">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ILZ3MuHE">我：……？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YYiglF08">这合理吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TQuwfBoG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AoMzY5iK">大师兄目睹了我惊掉下巴的全程，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RsY60N94">他弯弯的狐狸眼中带着笑意，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dZ4-Rxgm">拍了拍我的肩膀，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SdbhfbgM">说道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W-ZQDFK6">“师父他……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OHfsNWRu">是个傻瓜，也是个天才。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JHfnhEkn">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Qu6Aemrl">二师姐也站在一旁，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-exkU1NC">冷艳地点了点头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ITs65eQU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zbZ-wCjU">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nwnoumt8">可恶，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Fd_TBiI2">这个傻瓜居然是天才！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vQhdTs7H">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sEQsLjU7">看着师父在绿竹林下挥长剑时翩若惊鸿的身影，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mnW5Pb8-">我决定留下来学剑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Sv61d-wd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RhAlT3pC">师父耍完剑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q0iA0AU0">走过来臭屁地向我炫耀：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f5bDgc0o">“怎么样，我厉害吧？你留下我教你！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ltaTfr6A">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DN2iYuOF">我点了点头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="abFDdDPp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pLyX4FB-">他笑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kj7WAfSX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ehu2h7QP">注意到我旁边的大师兄二师姐，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cqqjExdK">师父说道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xCPa0tmZ">“老大老二，你们怎么来了？正好，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XerIcKyq">以后你们就带带小四熟悉一下门派。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T0rg_3Wk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1ezG-Poz">大师兄笑道：“自然。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sdQIO8xz">二师姐没说话。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EbkuDXHM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OAjT-g2l">师父把长剑扔给我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qupJ5pXP">打了个哈欠，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OswyXPxr">说累了要去睡觉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6GpA3YWb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R-0OkZ15">我跟着大师兄二师姐巡山，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TFSG-J01">不知道为什么，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oE8zeNSY">说巡山好奇怪哦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ctQezgV3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jx94TjRc">长剑山林木繁茂，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mcsfgmXm">奇花怪草多，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WLdjvRd_">蚊虫鼠蚁也多。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_BCmhrgb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZJhwD79H">被叮了一身的蚊子包。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SmQGPdMG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N7IPo_Qd">大师兄二师姐安然无恙，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7H8u_v6_">很是同情地看着我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OV_VetMN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MeTVchQW">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_jA0jyVg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U_TGFB5E">蚊子很嚣张地落在我的脸上，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WQkwYLve">我面无表情地一巴掌拍了过去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kHkEh4zJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="v_BfVvaj">然后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mlRRKxYI">啪——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xpd5xFcq">扇了自己一耳光。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0MZ6m8e_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gDaHDBw_">好疼！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iG8CpDst">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="23Aq473G">果然，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jj8Vu6zX">万物有灵，蚊子除外！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oDWj0w3i">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="piBY0YnK">我怒了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vBQnKbPK">抽出双刀，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8JUdaxL3">要与蚊子决一死战。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="F4GDfhVd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HL2AhzQp">大师兄：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K12sKFwF">二师姐：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7GzT4NMw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WPh9w-As">我举着刀，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nsIy_Haf">盯着在眼前飞舞的蚊子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8zE0RRgL">突然一块紫纱布从天而降，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IDnXSEsl">罩了我满头满脸。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dfbuTVsN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XDGkKqMo">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rc4v6FyK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wNHTMM4H">二师姐冷声道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YxLfETl1">“盖住脸和颈脖。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vFAd3Io-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p8bPq3GM">我看向她，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CevMzjkl">发现二师姐赤着左臂。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6QCrBTM8">她把留仙裙的广袖撕开，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Vs8YU7cm">摊开就成了我脸上这块布。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oPn4G2c8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pGU1fSbj">我很感动，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wqXU6GWF">然后发现，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cKoHw08Q">师姐的手毛有点长。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Th9riJBs">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gPWhfxRU">继续巡山。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2ccpglRC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Usy_MXS3">遇到在后山种菜的三师兄。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RA_zGvZ2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eVQn2nfN">三师兄见到我们，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g5Tag6GE">放下手中的水瓢，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JP5ACgx3">点头示意，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CUhOkko0">道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j0W6N_4z">“大师兄二师兄四师弟。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pe0fvdIa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yQebq_xO">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TjuNSgSo">我看向了一旁身穿留仙裙高贵冷艳的二师姐。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WjTxCY85">什么二师兄？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ysmDxdnP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eE91KE8R">可能是我的表情过于惊讶，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SDKf5rBy">另外三人都齐刷刷看了过来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bCS1vaYF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OboApHFM">大师兄装模作样地拍了拍脑袋，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8flin24_">才笑眯眯道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ueJOMTG3">“对了，四师弟还不知……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g_Yyxbvn">二师弟是男子。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="X267HSyp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sXjB3e4k">二师姐，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wH7NdFCe">啊不，二师兄也转头看着我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iNDk1eE1">眉眼冷艳，声音难辨雌雄。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ad9zs1XP">“怎么，没见过男子穿留仙裙吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uVObSSLp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P1FVrKJK">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BQxzQK0j">的确是第一次见……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YcTQN1wk">而且你的伪声学得也不错……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6_QaWFwz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>8月31 吃枣药丸</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YLmG_aLW">唉，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KS2SCzNR">我没有想到，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BvbTssYE">师门里全是大老爷们，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eaXSm9qo">还有一个只知道吃饭睡觉的猪。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AYjHymPP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mRs2W9aH">终究是我承担了所有。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gUHyohzu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GMyQlSXg">正式成为长剑派四弟子后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u-qfGJsi">我每天的任务就是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="__25JaiL">下山赚钱，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yjZTq8mJ">养活一门派。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GwVITADT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JTDGzHUu">不要问其他人去哪了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1SpQCfKv">问就是死了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j8SvPd7Z">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vwDm-S0x">…</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aR6gvWHe">好吧，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oxvuN_H8">我在说气话。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p_NDjJJP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vwYAFlKd">主要原因是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RrIvkJWF">让大师兄二师兄三师兄下山的话，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j0pzW9g2">赚回来的那丁点儿钱，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oDyPO9vz">根本不够养活门派。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-FvPITVF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SPV67HRF">我很好奇，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="L8g0p5vI">他们下山都做什么去了？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ERBTPzHQ">每个人竟然只能带回来几文钱。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hoZjjDsx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ykllvayz">我问他们：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RFNjwQoB">“你们，不会真的去讨饭了吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i6XK8GlC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V2s_tM2D">静默。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jv09MHFl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OPu5xhqZ">良久，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nR_a_51y">大师兄的笑脸有一丝龟裂。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UPHmLzmI">他说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s6bxxZFf">“难道……你不是？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p7UNAST6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LkUI398K">我：……？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wWtsicco">当然不是啊。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P31BCNrS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5u3t6mFu">二师兄先是一脸茫然，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rZY4Rl0E">觉察到不对劲后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iFTz2Yqj">艳丽的脸上也绷不住了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9wGoS52_">他咬牙切齿地问大师兄：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vFZ--wpb">“谢、宵！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HpqKKHKw">你之前跟我说一般人都是这么赚钱的！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ENCTLN0B">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g9mfsMAd">大师兄试图维持笑脸，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VIKxalsA">指着三师兄，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="45z8xP4N">据理力争道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rY1u-227">“我没错！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PlDOa5uJ">老三就是这么干的！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1SwrjZuM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dh5ucE6s">三师兄捻着佛珠，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cBp1lMQr">满脸疑惑：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sgdK-gtW">拜托，他是个和尚。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H9ENfVGO">去化缘不是很正常吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bxtbN_8_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4zPpA3xG">我不可置信地看着大师兄二师兄，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gRRd2QfB">问道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="S1W-qIJE">“你们俩……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qBhpoDw0">不会学三师兄拿着钵去要饭了吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hJ1IyEsm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-0mqrTS7">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EipWjMHg">空气中飘荡着尴尬的气氛。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9QVAgDsG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JraK0jGk">大师兄对我笑了笑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dXyY4vbS">展开折扇摇了摇，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AC4Jzfy8">说了句天气真热，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="b9_6yxKg">就转身走了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RvfaLFQu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="piS0X6hS">二师兄从留仙裙的广袖中抽出一根长鞭，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ov6IB6lV">追着大师兄边打边骂：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kjAABjcm">“谢狗！你敢诓我！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="F0MTVX-5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PSZNFxww">我看着追逐着的两人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jXM1wpJJ">心中大为震撼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ci8ko-p7">……？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RaYSMcgT">真就，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xhcgSc_N">一个敢说，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Dv_SeRat">一个敢信。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uFnZpeEU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G0MYVkyy">长剑派，吃枣药丸。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>9月1 下山赚钱</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kDroEpJ2">二师兄追着大师兄，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TQ8-097t">绕着山头跑了三圈。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EMXD9XrZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HIeODnhP">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="S6w99z1u">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5cQ5Xauj">三师兄：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Jz0Dm9P6">“阿弥陀佛。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wBPnedlb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ttBQwjt7">我无语地看他一眼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Fnm3aFqE">别装了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6X1QKVBp">你微扬的嘴角，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Dvf_XOn4">充分暴露了幸灾乐祸的内心。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2a0DVIzK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eGq3wSLr">我问三师兄：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7hvIDFZJ">“咱师门这么穷，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="plCsUslm">那你们都靠什么过活？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="drvIIqz1">吸收日月精华吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OfvB-E-a">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K25FHJSH">三师兄委婉地表示：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h9xUHMXp">“后山有一块菜地。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VEhlz2ED">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JgLFjvjP">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8F9cqKK_">难怪师父喜欢睡觉，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="20ezQMAm">原来是节约能耗呢。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0tIT-oDT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="L5Gofezl">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OUgOm_HE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mo4R0CkW">新的一天。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zTv7sXBJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="atLqrslN">养家糊口的一天。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lKsaoB_a">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UgCDNAeV">我 召集了大师兄二师兄三师兄，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nSTwTzuL">然后把师父从洞府里揪出来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4-BQSRDx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZSpKoZDB">师父的头发永远乱得像鸟窝。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pRcCO6qk">他嘟着嘴含糊道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vB5C2nzT">“小四，你叫醒我干什么呀？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Hg9IKp19">人家还没睡够……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8XSVyvp7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f-mI7jt-">说完他跟没骨头似的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xvUAKk2N">软绵绵地靠在我身上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OZzxj0KE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yZ_KkDXJ">我一个左移，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bJeHLOzs">师父面朝着地，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9BMvvgUs">摔趴了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="41Y3V534">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-381YTh6">二师兄关切地问：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="npWYkiOE">“师父，你没事吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8T1x2JEX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IvMP9K_T">师父的脸还埋在土里，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HyyJRSAk">仰起头说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qdKVs1ti">“没事。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KO0fd0Zk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RlAwwH63">“这样啊……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7QLlEMB6">二师兄很遗憾的样子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J-eUYOLq">于是提起裙摆，上前踩了师父一脚。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NQMZNSyL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zGGQBddT">师父又趴回了土里。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m9cxupkq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OQCEtTSS">大师兄笑出了声。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ApQHjRZK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-ENKwsGy">我&amp;三师兄：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mLjDiIbY">真是师慈徒孝。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kcRlJ203">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="efEfUh_z">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Pxo9RpBo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J8FlF5AP">“好了好了，不要闹了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cxgJSArJ">我把师父挖出来，拍了拍他身上的土，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0yMxXsUH">正色道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GUZAyb1V">“今天有正事。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CME16Fv2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AMb5vozQ">我用目光扫过他们一个个的脸，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ThJyBhI9">说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="E_AnrSlP">“大师兄二师兄三师兄，你们今天随我下山，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G-vNH3B2">学习赚钱技能！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2JjARUly">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ys30fSql">师父像个小学鸡一样举手问：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QmyOcsZT">“小四，我呢我呢？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="72jnGfpQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="85aS6LlE">我按下他的手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q9dRn9q7">“你去给后山的菜浇水松土，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eC5gAUHa">实在没事干就去把大粪挑了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YaoB-D59">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wFS-laBm">师父抓着我的衣摆，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5wjAyDOr">嘟嘴撒娇：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iSRk17eX">“啊……我不要去……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KYv9L_be">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Cn5QaeYi">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1VUFHjrh">莫得感情.jpg</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wwvCWBKe">抽刀。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Cwn4SkZ4">“再嘟嘴把你嘴巴割掉。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sosAk3CD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BJuEi6ca">师父：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yMllVeOF">哼！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hqwVe6Bz">他气成河豚鱼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6TAtgNiu">鼓着脸向后山走去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2fgpEyX_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FG97qlKH">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8JD23e5p">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iTNbeTzW">带着三个人下山。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XnnDT0xB">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MKQSbKRj">顺便在山腰捡了几块石头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iAXi7p42">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QRPONz03">去市集。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O_5ruuvL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T5q-pJUR">一路上不断有人指指点点，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T3NLkt3S">“就是那几个……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r5_y6qke">有手有脚长得一表人才衣着光鲜……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_EqP2Jxm">却经常来讨饭……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0Ao-W9mm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A7C8kO4e">我有点无地自容，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k3CiotfG">想让跟在身后的三个人滚蛋。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WX8FCbtz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k0y1qCuS">忍住了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_3wP7TTk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LPV1N2Ef">到了我往常来摆摊的地方。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FExbU6UL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qhI4qbIe">让大师兄二师兄三师兄站一边。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fG-RYQLz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="urCEAOI6">我熟练地吼道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NBpADVxo">“各位父老乡亲——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P__s-Gdy">有精彩表演——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qKM2x1iU">走过路过不要错过啊——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Eip8jqoh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uYkBsL45">很快就聚集了一群妇孺老少。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Dz8Y7iji">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HY21H_Mv">今天，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jBNkC4-u">我当众表演了一出胸口碎大石。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hSq2ER0R">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z4br2cyz">围观的男女老少喝彩道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R4-hSnRp">“小伙子真不错啊……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hvRDEHP6">“这石头是真的……碎石飚到我这了……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5RxRc0b6">“厉害呀……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LBVZwQ9h">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PJekwr4X">收到了不少零零碎碎的铜板。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="__4dHw2B">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ilgLXlOW">我捡起铜钱，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QN1-FqqS">回头对师兄们露出了八颗牙齿的微笑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="X-K5kANN">“你们，学会了吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5Qs7KIdo">来，试试看！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O86j9flr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HH2u7Pwf">师兄们：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="syhsRwti">“你嘴里有血……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OzQNyZjB">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>9月2 遇旧识</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Y9LPuWn6">哦，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="761uCOWi">原来是吐血了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LJ1u1IiZ">难怪嘴里有点腥甜。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ijHHdnC1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_kdjA9fa">我用手背擦了一下嘴角的血。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RkNsGowA">“小伤，不碍事。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iio5HOId">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2lZrbiqM">咳咳咳咳咳咳——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="06vOaYIy">哇——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-PC_9zwJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U3kosdNO">呕出一滩淡红色液体。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IAw19XQf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JokIxRb5">大师兄二师兄三师兄：！！！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t0fsCfix">“四师弟，你喷血啦！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YUi0nRnj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I6BQNdXS">这三个人猛地冲过来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AyKF7nY3">扛起我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3rJeXqXK">像搬一条咸鱼一样，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-jOshVak">将我搬到了医馆。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ms0DhgRV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Gm1BniWZ">我还没来得及解释一下，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P-yyopLk">可能，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k8Ffl8G3">那只是口水和血混到一起了……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r_-4Wnaq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SJq2c6d3">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vKZ5SSu4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YyXJmJZ8">医馆。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PxtZu9Jz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="w-fn-BzE">师兄们扛着我夺门而入。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YyNCW9O_">“大夫，救人！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EPQiBOdD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="efOQMfKP">医馆里坐诊的老大夫都被惊到了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RnSG97dn">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8-YgNpqw">我挣扎着下来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SjryF_I3">对师兄们解释：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QVNOhd7v">“我没事……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kzYl4bSx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MfyVWWyJ">二师兄打断我的话：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="19NrCya9">“不，你有事。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Go2eDon9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZJ1puKq1">三师兄对老大夫说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2IO1AgTN">“我师弟受了内伤！吐了好多血！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uj-abRwg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8wXGgJiQ">大师兄补充道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i88xkdkU">“可能命不久矣！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PPTizCJN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="THjR6nk9">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f4JOzsAb">你们就不能盼着我点好吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2vKIi5PL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_b-ui733">行叭，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4N_2B_i5">那就看看吧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B5UZx9OL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PnjEID0K">老大夫抖着干瘦的手指，给我把了很久脉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uN_0H1cG">他皱着眉头，反复地看我的面色，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PRP13XYb">又是让伸舌头又是扒眼皮。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DfiKwp_9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EnuFAGnk">许久。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FQjZmVjA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BnF6LbTj">老大夫收回手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oU62LRAV">摸了把胡子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G4wxzJnd">开始摇头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LGkBO4Qa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gxaVLI7e">看他这架势，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VP2AVp4M">我突然有点拿不准，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5Cdx_Bbb">该不会我真的快死了吧？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EMiva42_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4kCVElBZ">三师兄似乎从大夫的摇头中领会到了什么，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sMXN0wFp">他捻着佛珠，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="butLrJ0i">垂头道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3_GzLYRZ">“阿弥陀佛……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o11kawsH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GLG7GeG7">大师兄二师兄开始叹气。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0gRloAyH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="49B-iTGY">我咽了咽口水。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dYNkS7g0">……？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3GeIXmoD">我……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n6QRNbVi">难道要死了……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5BLP9nD-">不会吧……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U0cNtCuJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QFBlNgEL">老大夫斜睨我一眼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Hidf2Z9P">缓缓道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NchWY5vN">“内火旺盛，齿间溢血。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AYu5L-Ej">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6JhDnGIB">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="izE2Ym0F">哦，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8hHFKpQR">就是说，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MPBGEZRL">上火，牙龈出血。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pgAXnKNf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vtPCdPuI">“上火……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LkB-3ZpX">噗哈哈哈哈哈哈哈……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_gDIpfro">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PT2Yy1bk">耳边突然响起有点熟悉的笑声。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ozMKFPxn">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6NsO9y_f">不是师兄们的声音。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7ZkxnqUT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lvzqOSro">我循声望去，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SL8JppWX">看见了那个不知什么时候混进来的人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RdiGyAjn">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AgQdVZ0Q">他扶着门框，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GGyvk5fN">笑得直不起腰。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iuusb6Sm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0dpz05W3">是南竹。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4cOf0kMq">——</p>
 <h2>9月4 暖心</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ojZsqDUQ">南竹，卒。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2gcLhNZe">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ytlc7uwG">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7rmLTW8q">假的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="65rInmG-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dm2NOe0_">师兄们的目光也落在了南竹身上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EpioVJjq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J8oJMyYJ">这三个憨憨秒变正经。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CKQ276wI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WSF1z6ec">二师兄眼中寒光一闪，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iZLamNFG">长鞭一挥，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yACBXtQS">将南竹捆了个结实。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gTwya2S_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ojpgq595">南竹被扔在地上，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wLqcqGiT">像一个裹好的粽子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l0nP9Urc">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5KxooSei">大师兄半蹲着，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qUVe3iqK">用扇子挑起南竹的下巴，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="klyu59QV">审问道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HlL-zmFI">“你谁啊？什么人派来的？谁给你的胆子笑？知道我们是谁吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uHJsBQMe">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IlSkprhw">我：......？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2EE4bug7">师兄，你们怎回事？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y0PR7dVL">咋突然就切频道了？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="F_W-G2tc">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bEv5RLg4">南竹没有说话，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vhY5f0ST">因为二师兄把他的嘴也绑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="75v2d0te">“唔唔唔唔唔唔......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CxjbHfnh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LJbKI0l6">我没有帮南竹解围，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ARXxGa1s">只默默地看着他在地上打滚。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ELByVDG6">哈哈哈哈哈哈哈哈哈哈</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RKETifYq">他这糗样我还是第一次见。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LDL8U13L">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s7nCQM9Q">唔呜呜呜唔唔唔......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="11hMb6Xd">他还瞪我呢。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BauWBtHK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6ni1MYz6">我捂住嘴，不然怕笑出声。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dPbKgaIy">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MlYfVNAl">正当我想多欣赏两眼南竹的糗状时，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0eHj4eE3">三师兄说话了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KSYbslTZ">他说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BSW1SWaT">“二位师兄，这般对待这位公子怕是不太好吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bRODEfec">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Qw3uoWoE">我收了笑，摇摇头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tbZtPOo2">到底是和尚，心软。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hTzqY6XO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5BPByc4C">大师兄收回扇子，应和道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7BZ7Pt_e">“老三说得对。那就......厚葬了吧。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g1kea2vo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AVZNCs9w">三师兄点了点头，光亮的脑壳闪着神圣的光。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SXR_qUPN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C7EIYJ05">我：？！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="onwFMPjC">你们认真的？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="99VqNiXj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qvLBZG6b">说话间，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_0gCA1bY">二师兄撸起袖子，已经麻溜地把南竹抬起来了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="85hcnVt5">他说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OdFU6g71">“长剑山山腰还有几块地，埋那里吧。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t22KPN6L">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PRKHNL0W">我：！！！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Pu1wY309">“等等，别走！师兄们，这没有必要啊！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aigwvG-M">我坐不住了，起身拦住二师兄。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Do6jlN_m">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mMdHy9ez">谁知这几个人充耳不闻，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mgPzeuVW">仗着轻功好，绕过我飞一般地扛着南竹走了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rlHekQVU">只留下我伸着尔康手。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ezBB460J">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f25ZLr1D">我：？？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_ZQXjvYh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sH9BWyGp">正要追上去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GoEfEr3-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TbwA7B7_">被老大夫逮住了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5s9Wh4da">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kLEbpe1b">老人家堵在门口，神色庄严。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pBmZwb5Y">他向我伸手：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8lh4GUUg">“看诊费。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AZYqJP8l">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t548CrjO">我：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OQL725PV">看着老大夫伸到面前的手，想起我只有一丢丢钱的荷包。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Pl0v9RZt">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3xoP7TSO">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z-gc9ykC">电光石火之间，我突然悟了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7kBcSQmD">师兄们为严惩嘲笑小师弟的人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RmMafwk6">不惜杀人灭口，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="01NylE4K">背后的原因令人暖心。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TmNle3N9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ge6CiB5y">他们只想找个理由跑路！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WYeTAZOq">可恶！</p>
 <p data-pid="O6fYWq8l">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>9月5 打工</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GI3sNVxT">不够钱给看诊费，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MYdP-SI9">被留在医馆砍药材。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xsYTqCXi">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I0W_cCKg">砍了三天。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LKEkjuYm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yPpe1Slh">其中有两天在摸鱼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Wzq50CVF">逗老大夫的孙女玩，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CwR_MaxN">撸他家的狸花猫。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2frV17Vm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3n9FzoR_">第四天，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tgRS-N15">我以为可以走了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1Jbp1KIA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qr5SsuUf">结果又被拦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2mt2k6rf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xHCTuE5I">老大夫堵在门口，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TEN7mfwi">问我：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="odnnGUD5">”小伙子，我看你人长得还行，做事也可靠，你愿不愿意做我孙婿？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="baiWGidR">他这语气，大有我不答应就别想走的意思。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6tPL73er">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4LSAj1Sd">他的孙女抱着毛茸茸的小猫，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MHt0vgFc">扑闪着水灵灵的眼睛，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LGAp9vtT">对我说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9aZbCbbq">“哥哥，你要走了吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5--lGAYc">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Bl6u4cBs">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V8xDiFhu">老大爷！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qEf8zfrn">您孙女才五岁啊！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n-mGKNkB">要是答应了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qzvpECH4">我真就变得可刑，可拷了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nf8VSz0C">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aWU2AZWk">用沉默和他对峙。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3yx8sGuO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-rnnJjfd">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YtCe4Sgo">突然，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="F1kXbSqx">灵机一动。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8Yt4DEBb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JCr1-P4L">我轻揪一下小孙女的羊角辫，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WwjCs9Ap">问老大夫：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cj3mGq1U">“非得成一家人才可以让我走吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LHheQ1Nw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IH_vtcre">他点了点头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="E1YSwrl5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lZpkOtOq">行。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kFUjYV7u">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B-H3qVam">我啪一声跪下，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R75jhGER">冲他喊了一声响彻云霄的</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sg0LLM_X">“爹！！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-Maq0dM3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ESm_mPhm">老大夫：……？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pz6FrRVA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ektRegCJ">“喵呜~”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H2EkvsTK">小花猫大受震撼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9Qv07lsO">跳到我头上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="adJKXPjD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oz8gkkpr">老大夫差点气晕，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ueCYpWZz">回过神来就要拿拐杖抽我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PpvT1Pag">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KYdyHvgd">拐杖没落到身上，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jceSlhSJ">我只感觉到腰身一紧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3nQ6ZK5l">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T7wdY9xV">小孙女突然冲过来抱住我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5t-_rGGN">娇滴滴的声音带着哭腔：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="naofV6_Z">“阿爹，原来你是阿爹！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YSOXvVfO">你怎么才来找囡囡？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T1tb8tel">囡囡都快忘记阿爹的样子了……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JQlzsT_8">呜呜呜……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zcRzT0oQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bXuGWEsQ">我：……？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Z2AvWGtz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Qcb0VjZq">不仅认了个爹，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="izf5VJRd">还喜当爹了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VpbtHEaO">这是我没想到的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5QFocilx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vbw4DeCm">老大夫举着拐杖的手僵在半空，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SVMutlkC">最终缓缓放下。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="psyrGzL1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rs3qw4kt">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dfwl2GGc">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="axUprMK9">第二天，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FRBPwhFI">在老大夫的威逼之下，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XnN9p9gQ">我带着吵着要跟我走的囡囡回了长剑山。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-vHRlk_-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fIHqukVM">回山。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oQ1SpWgS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="715hktOq">没见着师父，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4WJXaY3p">八成还在睡。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Gp2MlA8V">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nub5ESXF">我抱着囡囡，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rxBDWQ7G">囡囡抱着小猫。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DWdqqVlu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vA7ITWdW">迎面撞上二师兄。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ri1HjB9f">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ma3MWW1p">二师兄见了我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Gh7PeniY">咻一声后退了三尺。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FVlw_4ns">心虚道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xPqf1yGL">“四师弟，你回来啦？怎么还带了个小娃娃？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KIjssUnE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zIeeAFjh">我：呵呵。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SPJLz26Z">小奶猫：“喵~”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WuMv1DZQ">囡囡仰头问我：“阿爹，这个姐姐是谁？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KZXrMYBv">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Rl6mK6bp">我还没回答，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nHDrwRfG">只见二师兄更惊恐地后退了两步。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4BggVr7k">下一秒,</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="60p8fa_3">他的喊声让长剑山为之一振：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AQ7vd6nQ">“谢宵！老三！师父！快出来！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="10PcYDip">四师弟带着私生女回来了！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ykk7evOn">——</p>
 <h2>9月7 为了追他</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="icPZOD6q">二师兄的惊天一吼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nwxGyBQD">把长剑山上所有人都炸了出来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mMsiq8Re">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ph5kwEVT">好家伙，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n7osqjkR">这一个个人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AmmnbNG4">简直跟闪现似的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YNCRifkw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PKi3ZqEw">师父哭啼啼地跑出来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V4HIYAw0">见到我怀里到的囡囡，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xXMwuMRK">于是声泪俱下地质问我：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tgCA42qZ">“小四！你怎么可以这样？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Cg7WBPV8">这是你和谁的孩子？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FGdFGyNc">我不同意这门亲事！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="thkO7n2I">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="S4JRluVP">我没有搭理他。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-gGoXUlx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZGpltCq1">大师兄和三师兄好奇地靠过来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WeFvdyZ0">凑近囡囡仔细观察。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RHUIVI3_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yGkmfPVW">囡囡指着三师兄的光头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G4HJJ9DZ">咯咯笑道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RWyOg6pT">“阿爹，看，卤蛋！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R28Sgbi3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dQsqfYS4">我看了过去，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9Ah_F7EA">噗哈哈哈哈哈</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GL1MG416">本来不想笑的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bLjRPZhB">但是忍不住，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qrGvcZWU">实在太像了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g_C-QnJL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UiqkE81g">三师兄也不恼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RXdwNnPw">笑呵呵地让她摸头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="988NQeGy">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8ZU2n8iZ">我放下囡囡，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aq5-DJ4Y">看着几个师兄同她玩闹。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uVYlF26E">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FuQ_VN-8">就挺无语的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RdPciDsM">你们接受得挺快呀。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sL8uogKY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oB2S9F9H">也是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_iW9LtCs">小可爱谁不喜欢呢。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lkRTLLeL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O6SRgQFn">师父擦了眼泪又趁机靠过来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Rkr0g9m5">他看一眼在那边玩闹的囡囡，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jbSEcnzD">又看一眼我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mESAxv5A">装作语重心长道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rgyVSPe5">“小四，听师父一句劝。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WlDyOa1b">成亲这种事，水太深了，你把握不住的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BnopwNgw">要不你……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Xwpeiikv">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A5f87hx2">编，继续编。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7QZsanOC">我就静静看着他，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j9D3-0pT">像看一个傻子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kG_kXHsf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ifPiXYrO">师父说不下去了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C_73-b7v">开始嘤嘤嘤嘤嘤地耍赖。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5-jhh_YY">“我不管，你不许成亲！不许有孩子！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LkX0kg-u">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OgQNoa4F">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mPtK-fw_">傻*。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G_EU_bz9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GK94GfgH">我说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DIBaJPA-">“我哪能突然冒出来一个这么大的孩子？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A4DpQ9DT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2jc6jCh3">师父简单的大脑构造不足以让他马上理解我这句话。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1_3thivd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SKC01E5Y">这时，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n_uKEQxi">那边在逗囡囡玩的大师兄突然走过来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="v-W9IZE4">表情欲言又止。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lIrvq8zS">他对我说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s1ZU0FHL">“四师弟，那娃娃可爱是可爱，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="32qzHxNB">只是……长得不太像你啊。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SVQNhSUp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FIAu2iuz">废话，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bDJZZFtD">像才怪。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nmCO8JiW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LYa58Hj4">师父听了这话，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xJQR3j0J">却仿佛捋清了头绪。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dlCOlM_D">他恍然大悟道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Of-qjQVU">“原来如此！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UauxjhK7">小四，你被绿了！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4qyqS5Ti">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x4kryqvV">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="79X097Lc">闭嘴。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZJ_iuj_R">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pDtYf0Hn">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pVjyFTKD">——</p>
