 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ORB-p9Az">趁着囡囡和小猫玩，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aBUXbNCE">我三言两语地解释了她的来由。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="InJtO4ji">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RkkXcpMK">师父好像松了一口气。（？）</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0nBQQAD4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bSlL6QgY">大师兄二师兄三师兄听到我在医馆打工时，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cohpG8Xe">表情一度十分心虚。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mWQcQMc7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sir-9JzH">哼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eFb83WC-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rhojQ_k6">我想起南竹，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OQ7ijgib">于是问他们：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gjZnYd6t">“上次你们抬走的那人呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I3UjgrPB">总不能真埋了吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4ygWqXWP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a51lrfBV">大师兄看向了二师兄：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pJiYvLkG">“他啊。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AvShnKOx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8PSK1Nuv">二师兄看向了三师兄：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cIR8CtFj">“我们看他衣着奢华……像是富家公子。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ozLRwljy">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dcBj2QRY">三师兄咳了一声，看向师父：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TI1rsE9J">“所以……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nGtqjBc8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0qAJ0SAm">我：！！！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="27rcWDyn">你们不会杀人劫财了吧？！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ALknXnq2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fTbN6KuU">师父不明所以，憨憨地歪头道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qq4HW9Wm">“你们是在说小五吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H1okP5Vi">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Xohjp1a_">我：小五？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZrwnVViJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MLJ0YkvT">三师兄继续说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-26HTl_I">“所以……让师父收了他做弟子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rSF9reje">现在咱们都靠他养活了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tC5XSJ09">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G4vIILYC">我：？？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7WJcH-Dg">震惊，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qYH3TbXY">追求对象变师弟。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XmI2AeYD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YvQbzPSs">师父问我：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W9PXN4yT">“小四，你和小五以前认识吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eWzaLFJD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1wquaKQT">我挠挠头：“这个嘛……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Do6X5dwL">我学长剑就是为了追他。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nXvZUOej">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="922qbwmZ">师父：！！！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0Ih6a8DP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>9月9 走，下山</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5L5isJyG">师父的面色变得很奇怪，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HOrV3cjP">绿了，白了，又绿了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3csH38KE">衬得头上都带着点绿光。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="we0vZkUU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bUXAJRVO">大师兄极为八卦，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="369nI_v8">扇子一展，遮住半张脸</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cYMTxNO4">鬼鬼祟祟凑到我面前问：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-pE4AsSM">“竟有此事，师弟快快细说。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sDoIi3VF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pRpaChC1">二师兄依旧冷艳，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kuSwkyVx">但我看见他悄悄向这边侧耳朵了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EjzNmJna">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A2mRMKYC">三师兄的眼睛和他的脑袋一样在发光。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="71SmWaol">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UYgn583I">我扭过脸：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V-5nIdLD">“哎，说来话长……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NHZzq1tv">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o3_10esX">还没开讲，师父突然出手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MVFfHTuL">挨个敲了三位师兄的脑壳，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jSeVN3-b">咚、咚、咚</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EEigTIGb">他斥道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gO0PpZFH">“一天天的就知道八卦！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eT3vnzZc">没事就去把后山的菜地浇了！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N8W0dZo8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zpMslPWN">大师兄：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k4kIIBIV">“五师弟不是在浇菜吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mWUuXOvW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mbRHwULh">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8hcML_Fx">原来如此，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NrcbEYI-">南竹在后山。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QPPUmYxP">我把囡囡和小猫交给三师兄照顾，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cusV-O8_">决定去找南竹。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M18igFzj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sg5UQcMd">师父伸手拦我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ieTq9pnL">他叉着腰说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jsys0o2p">“不许走。哼，你们听好了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LrplZMzb">今天起，我要小五逐出师门！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3KOGkq6r">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NsdmNIg4">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gf64y4cx">你收徒是闹着玩的吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O56IfY6b">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DXAjxxNm">他的话音一落，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0u_zKfQy">大师兄二师兄急了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Jdy6K3Rx">围上去劝说道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2CfBSAOw">“师父，三思啊！像五师弟这种有钱又好骗的冤大头不多了，错过这个村就没这个店了！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HJp23Coi">“对呀对呀！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V7wU-BIZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="70d0vdP5">我：……？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RYuRVtqj">不得不深思，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZwUXX5S9">我当初到底为什么会拜师成功。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-aze6gzl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KnUaXo-8">趁机溜走。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a8VUYSpv">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FBcoHyu7">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DGFf68wI">后山。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i54V9AvU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="quCvGpdx">我看见南竹在锄地，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rwOxfUyW">不时停下擦一下汗。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ca5JWisv">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vieXH-32">真是难为他这个身娇肉贵的公子哥了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mOa3czrO">不过他为啥会肯锄地种菜呀？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BgdObUXs">疑惑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XnToNT3G">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7BA2Ct5t">我没有出声，直到他抬头看见我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2j5VnY42">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DfYepBrc">很难得的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qFvAQtwZ">他见了我像见了失散多年的老父亲一样，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7r8zmtiG">哭唧唧地冲过来抱住我的腰，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OYFtLfUp">一把鼻涕一把泪说道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zZeAhJOL">“朱珏！你是来救我的吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5EE1jRqN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LespKGMD">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7sNuAB68">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ENIYSk0l">哇哇哇哇哇哇哇呜呜呜——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YTpgSaj8">南竹哭了半天，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VN5qIGzL">鼻涕眼泪都蹭我衣服上了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QB2_nRAX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IWK6B8_t">咦惹，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="egvQETAh">恶心心。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3882ZeeB">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="km57u9Tp">我把人扯下来，问他：“到底怎么了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eCFjA4VW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kOKbif-J">南竹眼含热泪，控诉道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jMrnYyNI">“呜呜呜我被绑架了......他们让我拜师，还让我锄地......不然就要杀人灭口......我在这锄了四天地......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h8Y2cqwi">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0AdZVrUS">我：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FjL7hQFF">的确像是长剑派说得出来的话。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1YWdpoNR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wJKtSGbk">南竹可怜兮兮地把他磨红了的手掌给我看。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tukvk9wu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QiR1d9AW">我：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JXNBD0o2">“咋，还要给你吹吹不成？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xrAT4zxb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RtlYvB2W">南竹悻悻收回了手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_NLS91Ad">可怜巴巴地看我：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fufGO-t_">“我不要待在长剑山了，你带我走吧。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zzfRGX_w">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BINwiTkx">我想了想，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t0eps0_e">告诉他一个好消息。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TV4DUZDi">“师父要把你逐出师门，你应该可以走了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TIq5Tib6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B7y2AXp4">南竹：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q2uY_tO9">“当真？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rvDt32nB">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Lv-3NQ4b">我点了点头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tJZ0NuIM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Hj0wcjIz">他擦了眼泪，转身就往山下跑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vgSD2viO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ULKF1OY7">看着他逃命似的背影，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Vd0BFy9H">我没忍心告诉他，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NMsmoGDA">其实师父师兄那群傻子多半是唬人的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wrzh8ZGv">真要走没人会拦他。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MleeN390">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sjsyqB_e">南竹跑了几步又回来了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="412cp_94">他说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZLeDUBtJ">“那你呢？不跟我一起走吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="v5gWM7C3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yZD2M5_h">我摇头：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j8h4aBR7">“不走，我要学长剑！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="54sEavsE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dnkxIDdE">南竹：“你学那个干什么？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XOfgL9H1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-q4g8ODp">我：？！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GeCcvLsl">“不是你说喜欢长剑的吗？！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q_C-nzc3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6EMT5TXD">南竹一副迷茫的样子：“哈？我说过吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G_sEtKj8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HSfGIvz3">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uIXd3IXN">怒气+10，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ShLfuZSG">我右手按住了刀柄，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1w49W6d6">缓缓抽刀。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FjTpCQro">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DnVqPvi8">但南竹没注意我的脸色，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zNBOLdv-">而是握住了我的手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6HCIRIm1">拉着我向山下边走边说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gQOkpoGQ">“别学了，跟我下山吧。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rVS2-w7n">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yVIRrwFs">没走两步，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="opuIX6Nu">我们眼前闪过一道残影。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8dpHpz8r">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RN-qpHcg">师父头上的卷毛全都炸起来了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3CvuitjU">他手里拎着竹剑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tGX-klNs">冷声道：“走？你要带他去哪？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HztwySMp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>9月10 管好你自己</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GCdYGqDv">师父提着竹剑一步步逼近，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fj1GVcB0">剑尖格叽格叽划过地面，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Kmb7M7Xl">留下一条蜿蜒的划痕。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Oc6lZDHf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4eAc99GR">南竹握我手的掌心沁汗了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iPasuG6p">手指在不自觉收紧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Vkp5MwL4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A-6twGzL">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9YT1MQLx">一把抽开手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WCdSZUxh">并且狠狠拍了南竹手背一掌。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Y0V9vF45">“抓那么紧干哈？老子手疼。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nSfoX7Hf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g7dfYK4n">南竹：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TJUvPMxO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="am4NxauH">师父闻言，脚步一滞，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ODfBNthM">顿时气势全无。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Iej7d02d">他又变成了嘤嘤怪的模样，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EJqg4oyk">噘着嘴问我，眼睛却在看南竹：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9saFDC3P">“你们要去哪里？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GNm0aHcv">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="25FcNj0v">南竹战战兢兢退了一步，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RgPaPCVw">嗫嚅道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1TzF82Vl">“不……不去……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RmPWe45_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Br70yT_w">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3V6ni_Zg">怂什么呀。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kpqLJU0g">我把南竹拽到面前，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="06kYTUDA">对师父说道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-8pdvjtI">“我要带他下山。怎么？你有意见？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FHKx7P7k">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZJ4xebLK">南竹：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hlycP_Tv">我害怕！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tl03vvXN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HCyo0UVC">师父：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JdzstaUX">“我不准！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TeQncR33">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qVm8HQUV">我看了师父几眼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qOj3hcMj">哪能不懂他那点小九九。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Caxk39Dy">于是，我说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qjDtrAv9">“你舍不得？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LIxfTUxg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EdBuBDSz">师父的脸刷地红了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_430tx1C">竹剑脱手，他扯着衣摆扭扭捏捏道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ngR542T0">“你看出来啦……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KG0UBdK8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uawpC7Gx">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NXEmmIzy">你脸红什么鬼？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0sxTbQZ9">我：“废话，师兄不都说了吗，错过这个村就没这个店了。南竹这种冤大头的确不多见，你舍不得也正常。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="brp2l0qG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="thT1-luM">师父：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rsUQsL8M">你阅读理解不错嘛。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tLmrfBTo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QQhtPBRv">南竹：恍然大悟.jpg</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aqQIgB49">“呜呜呜师父，你放我走吧！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RplzGaLB">强扭的瓜不甜！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DL7oukfx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z6s-WeeP">师父嘴角抽了抽，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WW0h6FM1">捡起地上的竹剑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yxXdK48C">“你再说话就别想走了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pICWW1Lg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wKAubSCk">我捂住了南竹的嘴。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="40gHpm3P">“好了，他不会说话了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XQz-SGdR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_ngMNKDK">师父：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="42vBtNGy">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wjolfJQE">扯着南竹下山。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="srYFaujH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HKK_-hqW">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lGrpiA75">师父在长剑山巅，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IzZXFIO2">远远眺着打闹离去的两人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sdhpPcG2">他捏紧了手中竹剑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="riV8-GJ9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xOVNdiHe">一阵风吹过，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uZBj0ANi">竹剑化作齑粉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kiTFztHF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ile0Q2QY">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A7m1buYB">带南竹下山，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iFB7K2mB">回南府。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KfMol_uA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Xul6WZ_5">南家是城中的大户人家，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BC8mWpSf">老有钱了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="becvThA2">南竹是南家矜贵的小公子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5YlsKDmT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uhrNW-zB">送人到门口。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qbfBBP5r">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kk7bbLEq">我抱着双刀，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WkYtpuLP">头一偏示意他进去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C137-GTT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3tR77uL6">南竹走到门前，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8Pk5QfLV">忽然回首：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lSAmqZda">“你送我回来，我爹娘定会很感激。你要不要留在我家住？再也不必漂泊……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iQbzMXLP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wqTSlXif">我摇头：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0A5sPpwO">“不必，我还要回山上。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="74lLG-ss">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3urkXSBD">南竹：“那个门派你回去作甚？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pwpkiZiZ">你不用去学长剑了，我……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nrnAcq2_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vyp1KVxN">我眯起眼看他：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7Lfwn_H2">“嗯？教我做事吗？管好你自己。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N_EXWbzU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gTcH-XjC">南竹：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lpjiOUdC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2OL9Vsbk">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="reEA2K2s">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wDocYY7d">回山。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tmzlVBt9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QZh1I_FM">师父还待在原来的地方，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zxZjSpwM">背对我蹲着在碎碎念。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vZtZnzAh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hJlagbUn">走近一看，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iZk1jGSA">他在用木棍数地上的蚂蚁？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fwtGZfN0">嘴里叨叨什么：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1FjIxfNo">“抢回来，不抢，抢，不抢，抢……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xZfaQiNN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B5iVS6XG">我走过去把他薅起来：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cQJR0PJk">“在这装蘑菇呢？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dH7m9GY4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Jy-m8o-u">师父手一抖，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2upfjNM4">枯枝掉地：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="902JhqKj">“小四，你没走？！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t7BfdnYo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6V7-Wx0A">“走啥？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Wu0Qcmh7">我说过要走吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fKOjdPXB">何况囡囡还在山上，我能去哪？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eTGVE2HX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>9月12 绑发</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uF4gqOQG">老实说，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QVtlL4yH">我不走只是因为还想学长剑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ic_MhXVE">绝对不是舍不得师父师兄们。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Fc8ls2Oj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ch01C40y">哼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XtpO2Zd1">谁会舍不得嘤嘤怪和傻瓜啊？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ddzDQPLr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tb3PWVtZ">去三师兄那里找囡囡。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SRq12tvR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q73TrUtx">小家伙玩得可开心了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_IZHt985">和三师兄一起逗小猫。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PLCCJRja">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QH-Vqryu">囡囡一见了我，就奶呼呼地喊：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lT_21xI9">“阿爹！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZddhNF3r">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="e3mx8Ivb">“哎。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5M4IA_c9">我笑盈盈地伸手去抱她。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hrQ6rnn4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QD1_9HqP">囡囡：“阿爹，你什么时候带我去找阿娘啊？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KfYcsiKi">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oxBQVdVj">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p-yz1Vcl">我笑容一僵，蚌埠住了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kbRXBejh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WpjjUt8R">三师兄眼神游移不定。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A9TiS-o0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iYNLpFNz">可恶，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1XvCWXT6">一定是他撺掇的！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0T2eZC_q">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rA-47Anb">不行，得先糊弄过去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GuaaQl4L">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gw5W77lV">我摸摸囡囡的小脑袋，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Np0z7bPf">说道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vEtwUegO">“你阿娘出了远门，要过些时日才回来。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="E5YN7oZ5">然后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hqAb-6Zb">我狠狠掐了一把三师兄的胳膊，笑问：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nXwV2g8M">“三师兄，你说是不是啊？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-s45seQ0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qo3WWG6C">三师兄：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3PptSJCA">“……额，哈哈，对。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Sxl2yBrh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tr6GF_cf">囡囡的小爪子扯了一下我的衣襟，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ma_s9UD0">有些失落：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V3-ZP-xy">“阿娘怎么也出远门了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vd0SCZyH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="feAH8Vq6">我心碎了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MimEbmZT">囡囡这么可爱，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jmYmRjxr">怎么可以让囡囡伤心呢。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i-OLWRQO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N76Pkkog">于是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qH1mE_HN">我问她：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l9Bk95La">“囡囡想不想骑大马？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="agH9hQ5t">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cEpDLKLC">果然小孩子的注意力被转移了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Xc0t1M--">“大马？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KQIMrVYZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mhHM72-v">我笑了笑，目光落在三师兄身上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HdGEO_yn">继续说道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iIjAKhvD">“是呀，还是光头大马。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7iW9a34J">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UyzijGmB">三师兄：！！！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fDopupah">你们不要过来啊！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RcGOICFA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N9eOUsOr">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AVHf7Br2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_ybBtcwR">一刻钟后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uD-XFHwM">囡囡骑在三师兄背上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rPzf4Lzs">笑呵呵喊道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3B3MIjrl">“马儿马儿跑得快~驾！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kC9g3hui">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="te-Gy5mt">三师兄：咩~</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x3A5LWpz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-dm5mzC_">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fLLtia0N">马好像不是这么叫的吧？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T8iS-CkV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p_XlF-9f">三师兄一副乐在其中的模样。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9GBZ_v__">可恶，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9R5JenZ2">便宜他了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MpAWSOzQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="c2ZRD-pE">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mOCWf59B">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gTCQmJUj">回山了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i3oKEujz">我又开始学长剑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kPjl30eG">这次不是为了南竹，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xBLW-RpU">我想清楚了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FI806OlG">男人只会影响我拔剑的速度！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iLR0IEDo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kzndbCnU">大早上起来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OXpKRilN">我打发三师兄把囡囡送回医馆，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3bchgq8c">并承诺过几天就去看她。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yTSbJAzH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JtI5lGTv">然后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="siJzo7lV">我来到了师父的洞府。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g3JyoM27">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MUHttGXN">人还在睡觉，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wM5VYdAQ">他身上不盖被子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YPr0_T6k">而是把被子捂在脸上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nMGSdyk3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="anCgUT9B">我：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R918A1J0">别闷死了啊！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="glK9sT0i">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RZLAiBry">冲过去掀开被子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cULbw6q_">检查人还活着不。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7LWmudAD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kp7i_nGr">师父半掀开眼皮，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q-2XSbPz">看见我，咧嘴傻笑：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RDmoG6vm">“小四？你怎么进梦里了？嘿嘿……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jSaefDIf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ufUIGxaE">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JduwJDQn">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="niVpz6Wv">然后他把倏地将脸埋在我怀里，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K7xZ7K3V">像小猫一样拱来拱去，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dU9elGXO">呓语道：“香的。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9AU45HF7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ppbaQ-XK">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rHP9HSto">我特么……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3mWsyFgF">一拳头把人捶醒。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4aCHut9B">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QHZl_wLl">师父多了一个熊猫眼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QzbGRO3U">！！！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BttHypOS">他这下清醒了，瞪大眼睛，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u_pMvbm4">又凑近我闻了闻。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3AJpeXNA">“小四？我搞到真的了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7PZqvxiL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0zpZA8Y_">闻啥，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NoodP-wg">属狗的吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5siJjWe9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JfFBH7GI">我把人扯远了点，说道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gghjFz4e">“还能是假的吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="obLFY1xR">别睡了快起床，教我练剑！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BuzeNz3O">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="X_GhiSdU">师父闻言，突然抱住床柱：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wr2fxUks">“我不起！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9xLkfT6C">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0Lc6qyRS">“真不起？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OOKo4FVE">“不起！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AANaxp9K">“中午不做你饭了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EpQBM-fe">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AqqFYnIm">“哼！！！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vghgPnjS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QoTQ57MQ">我笑了笑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YCGPEh-5">小样儿，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wEIG3d8p">还治不了你？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hwgPsgRf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8cUTSWlp">师父穿戴好了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bh3W7ouh">挺像个人样的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P1DR6GRS">就是这个卷卷的头发有点出戏。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wWJX0vn9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jFUDA6dp">我想了想，拿来木梳和发带。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5P31z5uw">“把你的卷毛梳梳好绑起来。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="62kH9l0h">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BS8vsaeC">师父：“我不会。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NVj6mFST">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rk7U78iG">我手拿着发带和他对视。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OPoxL9VT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FWZmPKib">他也看着我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WjSJCw9S">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="S0ID0FvJ">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ofLsXT2f">行叭。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UNHDOfse">“坐下。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Y1iVLfMG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1Tyi87sM">师父端端正正地坐在石凳上着，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0369tD6I">我站在他身后，拿起木梳。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IDlKuaGS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RdO2SdX0">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vu3JUMWz">石芾乖巧地坐着，站在身后的人在用手指给他捋顺头发，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pX6jF0h0">那人微凉的柔软的指尖轻轻地摩挲过他的发间，像柔嫩的柳条拂过发顶。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9gmTGQ0R" class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B9ALpLK3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="42v57SkG">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ro87-HGi">梳好了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EDZW7NNs">我拿起发带，却犯了愁。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qbalQXLQ">给别人绑头发我还没试过啊。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KDNYMon7">那就……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1Vh8X4Ln">随心来吧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yxZ52Jea">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="29OJS_79">于是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uHtWLpbE">啊嗷嗷啊嗷嗷——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tTcsMtnW">师父的惨叫声响了小半时辰。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Za4BqDYp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l-oVROqT">最后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TdyUE5SH">我藏起了薅掉的几缕长发，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="akBUvg1c">带着歉意对师父说道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dbuSqDBK">“要不？我去叫二师兄来？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0E1E-Uco">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>9月14 练剑</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HOCGsYi9">找二师兄。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7XJWDtJx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qS1soCi0">二师兄说他不会帮猪扎头发。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J76D9qr3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xKsoJ_pM">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="naHPhLbj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Rj0Xm692">放弃给师父扎头发。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jPl2Ej_Z">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="__sbA8Gq">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Wc1yJQQC">练剑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uGJmMdk_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NJhYnJ7R">由于太穷，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mpLuFbub">所以我也削了根竹子当剑用。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0y6ZKHyU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5zTGVFof">竹林下，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k10rEvh3">师父手执青翠的竹剑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qldl4nYp">迈步提肘，摆好架势。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Cjg0c_6d">他说：“看好了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xo9fyYXj">而后眼神一凛，周身气势一变。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="32Qsno0N">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="taDlU0Ow">刷刷刷咻咻咻——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xVVGi-mm">他的身姿翩若惊鸿，飘若飞雪，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VrK3l3um">看得我目瞪口呆眼花缭乱头晕目眩大受震撼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VxIOo1Lv">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KtnncV-C">简单点说就是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="L86oAPP0">看不懂。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YeXXcayD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h69S0KmN">师父舞完一套剑谱，身影定格在最后那一式。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Pg9EoSw9">竹叶被剑气击落，纷纷扬扬，洒落在他发顶、肩头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n0YZx_Iq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Gb_6enz2">我承认，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JWxQB1Sj">有一点点帅。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3-sH7qNB">只是一点。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EDUQecIe">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aUYeqqwe">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K5IUWPoJ">三分钟过去了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W6crYWws">他怎么还不动啊？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YVK0DIV1">不会是闪到腰了吧？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QZ8rOG1Y">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tpPNMnfl">我在他眼前挥了挥手。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="066nW92B">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WYVEyZST">师父倏忽一动，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_xexkYDz">笑嘻嘻地抓住我的手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-mflRsog">问：“怎么样？为师的剑法是不是出神入化？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rtp8IBmP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kMJ-Izwt">我：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CDAnIoVd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Wado04M_">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Labw5aih">谢宵躲在一旁的大岩石后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DEm6_EfM">偷看师父教四师弟练剑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U4VzGCPf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4-USy27j">师父的身法快得看不清。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hEZMmqv5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Qh1I9i2x">谢宵眼睛盯着那练剑的二人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ww5eZmTN">手扯了扯身旁那人的紫色衣袖。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PZJEGplW">轻声道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DA2aufHf">“孟岚。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h7jSXot_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tCURAKFl">孟岚翻了个白眼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o7ut71Ee">抽回自己的胳膊，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wJiIlxNz">没好气地问：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="osEiMXyt">“做甚？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hD39w5qa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Z1BipMkZ">谢宵合起扇子，抵着下巴思索，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rPd066cn">他说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l0jjPCb9">“你说，有没有一种可能......我只是说一种猜测。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zpB7lHQl">......师父在对四师弟孔雀开屏。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DkorVmf_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="w_qW8KIS">哦？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0UXGON26">孟岚闻言，也扒着岩石往师父那边偷看。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="me-GAc-d">切——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CriRgueG">明明是在教练剑嘛。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CTKv0Q21">于是他摇头，说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q0rrs18X">“绝无可能。毕竟，猪不会开屏。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yWrx71zA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LjQCl-eW">谢宵一拍手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EFF7JSi0">道：“有理。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TS4yNX7H">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CMrd8z25">谢宵继续偷看，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6WKkreeZ">只见那两道身影逐渐靠近。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Oo-Zi3hZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LChceHT6">他品出些不对味来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0Ukaayvf">又说：“不对不对，练剑怎么搂搂抱抱的？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="36O-wF1b">你看，师父都摸四师弟的手好几次了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0rLUV6mC">喏，还偷偷摸摸摸人家的腰。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="maFMCgWt">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tk7H7vKv">孟岚：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hwmck7-R">“练剑，需纠正执剑手势，扳正身姿，不过是寻常接触罢了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6ntLDjYu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5k6jCd3e">“你真这么觉得的？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o0o1J1-a">谢宵嘴角微翘，猝不及防地在孟岚耳边低语：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FfhdZOUq">“二师弟，师兄也教你练剑，如何？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ay6rRAFz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8oPdXQJk">孟岚：......呵。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C1QyQGZP">他抽出鞭子，啪一声甩在地上，鞭子砸地激起的风刃割断了谢宵的半截袖子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mcRdSGPG">孟岚冷笑道：“还教吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Kg1zIrU1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vjVBgxgY">谢宵：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9yHgBf7g">“你赔我袖子。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W4YGO7jF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rFgdt9ey">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cTFaJXYE">竹林下。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vVHwc2TR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8rK3bTQ5">练了一上午剑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CsMYMCr_">浑身都是汗。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FSBIjI8S">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Kxp-JKNh">但我好像啥都没学到，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HYlcHzhf">反倒是师父的剑法越发精进了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2sG04mdR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="06ElCLcz">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p-95mROB">傻瓜竟是我自己！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R_QKZ2bC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SipOoi79">好生气。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GvyVYe4z">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CN2XS5QS">扔剑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Qp4arBID">不练了！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cAhlYPqS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KhhxxBMp">师父：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M-5DWUSE">“小四，怎么了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D5KBGiHd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yIsz6EKf">我：“学不会，不搞了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oclra1jb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nkSBnqyK">师父：疑惑.jpg</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4fTNG-u3">“很简单的啊，就是这样这样......然后再那样那样......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rccIubif">你看，这不就成了嘛。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IsxWklEB">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vSq6v66V">我：╰（‵□′）╯</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="umcW6Ggk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wSwpaUJp">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9ScOMPEF">石芾笑了笑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="73ziwb7G">摸了摸小四的头：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0Kvbhx8T">“不要气，明天我继续教你。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m6xZCvUF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>9月18 阿娘</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-N4I6biu">第二天，练剑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oPDxhoP3">第三天，练剑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Os8lhEZM">第四天，练剑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J6gYe3HC">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ClachFZD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MLP2PgSU">一个月过去了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GThY3EB6">我终于......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="raLIW5tt">明白了世上无难事只要肯放弃。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="klHcbTpY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZkB6e574">师父：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t_f2iMsP">“没关系的，小四。我会就好。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oISSEr0t">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7GZgRbGL">我：怒.jpg</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a5YtJBrU">瞧不起谁呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f68VII1-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UdFSVQV8">扔了剑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8-4Nk_Ub">决定下山散散心。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YWuOd9xH">师父跟着我，说也要去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="juU9qAK6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ytv4yCe-">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2etH50CT">下山。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kpz4bT2T">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EZigiTrm">逛街。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6n8vlchC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k-haRrEb">在兵器铺看到一把绝世好刀，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ueq3KKh5">狠狠地心动了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5a-eY7-f">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y3U0oZOR">没钱，作罢。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ppaPn1gX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BvdPA9VU">师父像八百年没下过山一样，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MGhiy-Uq">拖着我这也看看那也看看。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pw4wr4Qd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="re6IPFbl">看到卖油纸伞的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HuaD5CpF">师父问摊主：“你这伞，能挡雨吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KqrymWsy">摊主：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UPwSZjmt">“能。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M3QEookh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rP7xwFfp">“能挡雪吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Zxl0LnYA">“……能。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lybfrrhE">“那，能遮阳吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B98Iezfj">“……滚。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DW85TBKp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7SZ3yn7B">看到卖水果的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DjSCyNkE">师父拍了拍西瓜，问：“你这瓜，保熟吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MXarRiZB">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bH8CB38e">摊主：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tkjr5Qd7">“不保。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mBeOIAJg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZSVY4gmP">师父：“哦，那保生吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="isjLhVeQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1Nt6H9ZL">好家伙，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3q1o-ltP">我仿佛看到摊主血压条拉满了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jmGoG-6-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DGRJGa7Y">赶紧拉着师父走人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fwpw7uEd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uk8a0fCX">顺便去医馆，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fEX8lQ3m">探望一下我的便宜老爹和宝贝女儿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Uy9DHQDp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Hus7rJA9">医馆，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0AfiCirC">老大夫正忙着看诊。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UMQn_7EG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GebUSLXM">去后院。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Wzn8j-Wu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sFP1qrTG">我把刚刚买的一个小风车玩具递给囡囡，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CR68ac6p">囡囡甜甜地笑了：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z165Vkh0">“阿爹真好。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="w4R2COd3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-Cm7hScS">师父：嘤嘤嘤嘤哭唧唧</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u4BBmKrG">“小四，小风车不是买给人家的吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nD7pH_B6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FA_M6-_r">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HmrP-lm-">你今年几岁了？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vRUjZjRj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fUyHFDBu">囡囡圆溜溜的大眼睛一转，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-jWpC9Ps">蹬着小短腿跑到师父面前，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CNJwRl9J">小手一伸，风车递给他：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cuSffXkf">“哥哥不哭，风车给你。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YF5Z3YEW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7oOotCBe">师父受宠若惊，接过风车，说道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u1FsfyUt">“虽然……但是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YA56h1dr">你不要叫我哥哥。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0JYOtDve">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GoGUpqHe">囡囡：“为什么呀？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lJ2Ke_AS">师父：“因为我是你爹的师父。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lgy8qzYo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4iMQquJS">“师父是什么？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_JRxnic7">“呃……这么说吧，就是你爹要侍奉终身的人。”‘</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nM3ldXPb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iLEQa9E-">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1vy7saYV">麻烦不要说得这么奇怪。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q9VzLy1E">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B1yIVDXL">“侍奉……终身……？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kkN7lRry">囡囡倒是呆呆愣住了，连脑袋上的羊角辫都透着疑惑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DLJaK3-l">我正想解释，只见她突然飞扑过去抱住师父的腿，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qmx8yoYM">喊道：“阿娘！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OhFFppKy">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nQTyRsnc">师父：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-D_6bjv3">“哎。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uc-qTztp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RujQTO2V">我：？？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LzpMlYFw">你做个人吧！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JglIUFz9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eDfAufM6">我一把抢过师父手里的小风车，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iKJdIFDj">放到囡囡手里，哄道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HK9izIcH">“囡囡不要信他胡言乱语，哪有男子……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5FgIC9SG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W-dNED6m">“不是吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WDEP7ftm">囡囡眨巴眨巴眼，金豆豆就要掉下来了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JyGK-kRJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sE8xIwoO">我还没说完，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xQw4rFBE">突然觉得身后有一股极其危险的气息在靠近。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l8fCENIs">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kcxOfs5m">果然，老大夫不知道什么时候忙完了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1142h6BP">出现在我身后。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YQJzjM5Q">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3GaTeIVk">老大夫看一眼要掉金豆豆的囡囡，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xny9GcdM">又看向我：死亡注视.jpg</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o_pS7qXP">“朱、珏！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3b1dgUYI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mndRHqvp">我连忙一个嘴上悬崖勒马，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q9aisuAx">抱紧囡囡，改口道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SVEM89Ut">“哪有男子不能当娘亲的？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RNp4A6Ce">没错，我师父就是你阿娘！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FzOF9q8y">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jcvQTeyE">囡囡抱着师父的腿，破涕为笑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="idlAObUV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2Ksauwon">老大夫看见囡囡不哭了，面色稍缓。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pO5YqT07">过了一会儿他反应过来我说的什么话，猛地又抄起拐杖追着我打。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qQFsYPbu">“你都教我孙女什么乱七八糟的东西！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>9月19 骨折</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7M-yEITH">老大夫身体挺好，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-jmQj1Y4">估计还能再活五十年。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oE2ViEOK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fy3XdhHl">毕竟追着我绕院子跑了十圈，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0HXaX8l2">大气都不带喘的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qa0yaCQs">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="itTAhT9d">我累了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oope-Htx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eqN3HSab">我装的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yQX617tP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gsRYAG4Q">疾跑中，我灵光一闪，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rp-m0OeX">使出从师父那学来的蹩脚轻功，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JFlmdqhF">飞上了屋顶。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DjwkpTuu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hTf9mrHL">站在屋顶上俯视着老大夫，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fB8rSHDj">我轻蔑地笑道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_f23775C">“哼，有本事你上来啊。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qJOy1BZG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5JmB8Czn">囡囡双眼发光，拍着小手说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QdJnB3uJ">“飞高高！阿爹好厉害！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NJ4U2ci7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ABpuS1Dq">我摸摸鼻子得意地笑了起来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2Ify0M4w">小意思啦哈哈哈哈哈</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="03uVjDv1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TF44AF0A">老大夫：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CDZoBwcX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tT0MsabP">乐极生悲，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qzhtJ4Wb">笑岔气了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CXRmtwVM">脚一滑从屋顶掉下来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cnwdHCQc">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Xy6lXbow">我：！！！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jsl89kXR">我命休矣！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GhB4dD1r">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cyDT22S-">囡囡：“阿爹！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Knq6Bhy6">师父：“小四！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-fGONcn0">老大夫：“兔崽子！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="chxwX9Xg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GRs-Gjx3">坠落的速度很快，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EI7_h2Bt">我眼前一花，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vXQWHi-g">只看到一道飞闪而过的影子赶在我落地前迎上来想要接住我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YaxjwlYG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="01R7YO3K">是师父。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tN1nZZeA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W-iD0dXQ">碰——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_H4xiB4l">一声巨响</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OhSa60yI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MyzIezEQ">我砸在师父身上了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SkedjFHW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4W-sAdaB">我一点事都没有。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XVTsTFYZ">好感动，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KXK9HSI7">这是怎样的师徒情深啊，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dj0w5Vdb">我以后再也不说他是猪了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MEkINhLS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2YCYoEoy">师父趴在地上，奄奄一息，似乎有话对我说，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LOiaylgh">“小四……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3z1A7vFe">我忙凑耳朵去听。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1fCD3CJj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y3Z9IQ0u">他说：“小四……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lQvzFlth">你……该减肥了……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yfVLqEIX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="go45-jhD">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tCc3x8ky">你再说一遍？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iKSntD01">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V8BIpUPE">“兔崽子，起开！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N6ATYEXD">老大夫冲过来拨开我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_xWJxO3e">他扶起师父，关切地问：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8EQfdwB3">“这位……儿媳妇，你没事吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SPqh7p8n">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ihncaqQe">我：？？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N5prCZSA">老爹，你清醒一点啊！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qg4DY--a">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PtNA9mCw">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aIhaRuFk">师父手被砸骨折了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="awP08ZtX">躺在板板上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u4Vk_QEM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7FXqOLvh">我不太懂，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sKM_sCbn">为什么手骨折了人要躺着不能动。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mBg2Y_vJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3Kk5BPsd">老大夫：“我说要就要。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fMqPh6Xq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0ZQToFC4">我：……哦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iIT1cN3y">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NrmkdcgU">老大夫去熬药了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zfJc32tw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZqZgEQaV">囡囡趴在床边，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vqokZoIE">对着师父绑着绷带的手臂吹气。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R8Ji6th5">“阿娘乖，吹吹，不疼。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aoF5lvWJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OAvriJ9X">师父面带脆弱的微笑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zPGfE4ag">蹙着眉对囡囡说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ww-pIpVE">“可是还是有点疼。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pLTa4ZOO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0D1186X-">囡囡茫然。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HhsdTzIe">“那怎么好呢？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zbN0-dQ5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UyHvKsqv">师父把视线转到我身上，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P5UiBCHa">楚楚可怜地对囡囡说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jpuG3F89">“如果你阿爹给我吹吹就不疼了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WOVFheuX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zdXQ_H4U">囡囡恍然大悟，饱含期待地看我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jv7r1Hrd">“阿爹！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4NtLcrQQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="026Epmem">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ljeYi0-I">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sWedyU3w">师父举着手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Xg1ZkJnV">对我说：“疼疼，吹手手。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RQdlargj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0Oxv2hmy">我yue了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rP6r_a5g">叠词词，恶心心。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FZKFR4dD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-6MqjS6V">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qsC0HcIV">还是吹了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EJQFLf16">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="owvAJHWN">被端药来的老大夫看见，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hDZwc8VI">老大夫表情一言难尽。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N4mptqDj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="smwZxUwx">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lDGaaOQe">听我狡辩……啊不，解释。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>9月22 喝药</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KTUzYRqD">老大夫熬了一碗漆黑的中药，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="keWsRgn3">那味道，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KqEo6VIb">闻起来十分酸爽。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Zr5bgFLt">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JDVyOc9z">师父疯狂摇头后退，不肯喝。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UUD2XHcG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VVBvTD8g">我舀起一匙药，送到他嘴边，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="piQWdexH">微笑道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yYoPUOqV">“亲爱的师父，不喝药怎么能好呢？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6JjwG2eS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7okikpFS">师父：“苦的！我不要！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P_-Pi_Eq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="36P2cw9p">“这可由不得你！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EDnrHL_a">我凶神恶煞地捏住他的脸，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a5z8DuTO">“今天，你喝也得给我喝，不喝也得给我喝！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kUfvvfdV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XpbuYOR9">强行灌药。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="47z2L7hk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IRIANsNO">师父全程呜呜呜呜地被灌完了一整碗药。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cbEn0oyN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V1ba7kDs">真可怜呐，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_LPVi1wt">他哭得好惨哦，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="arSlS-XW">我都不忍心了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T61wR2K4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1foxRIDJ">老大夫：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="30vX2W7o">你嘴巴不要咧那么开再说吧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9CLXZziq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R9NVzq5U">我收了嘴角，放下药碗，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6WCWAqvj">摸摸哭得稀里哗啦的师父，哄道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TqsvRTQq">“不哭不哭，还苦的话带你去买糖糕吃。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s0-ZePNW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zDmqs7q1">师父眼含热泪：嘤嘤嘤嘤嘤哇哇</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qSNMB8x_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3XbpOafq">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7FmMsBmg">真的有这么苦吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8c0Ocp64">我不禁试了一下碗底剩下的药汁。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="svOpU1cd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NUTkNcMr">砸吧砸吧嘴，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q40CckyD">这味道……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HB4WSK3o">我皱起了眉头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pHzCsRsw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZEIvmj6u">老大夫冷不丁问我：“怎么样？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zsbTlehl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UP2oLm2I">我：“好像……有点熟悉。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TIvdiNi5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bLfTznVb">老大夫：“那可不，这就是你上次喝的去火药。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A539Cztn">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="re2tb-EZ">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-AWQ3q1v">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZzCt78VQ">我指了指师父，“他也上火？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qYueN9_z">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uXvhQm2y">老大夫捋一下胡子，摇摇头：“非也，是你上火。。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WJiNxPqc">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YDz7OSTe">我：？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zxuv1Oc1">“那我上火，为什么让我师父喝药？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U6XCF8V8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wUC1kjuQ">老大夫用眼睛斜乜我，笑道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uVVUfpa1">“我可没说，分明是你让他喝的。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zSBrvUNQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KuGjGq3Q">我：？？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="X4FIs0lT">啊这……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W2U3CwB_">你敢说你不是故意不提醒我的？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zSAo1F-V">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q4tsdTld">师父听了大夫的话之后哇哇的哭得更大声了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D8C7M8EE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RmWqr2Jx">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dBfq0dzo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dfYioaQi">为弥补失误，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GDIOXLn2">我给师父买了三个糖糕。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MClq2Sv6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xGWsDsb7">“你喂我，我手坏了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ywHE4JhQ">师父啊地张开嘴。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2oha30nY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ft1kXLd5">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uRFiBNSn">拿起糖糕，一口一个。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fRVDobHu">“爱吃吃，不吃拉倒。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZBfjXiAX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4-fcIN7F">师父：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q56Gq-ov">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rZnmnoV8">糖糕被我吃完了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OB7EJ_VL">又给他买了蜜饯。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LWEz3XOL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jX3Gpe56">这次他乖了，自己动手，只是时不时幽怨地看着我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2tnPq2F7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="20X2VB88">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HT4K18OY">“再看，再看我就把蜜饯也吃掉。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>9月23 孝徒</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1j5Xuw4T">师父在医馆养伤，养了六天。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DLShb-dw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ELoBr-Gv">第七天。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VZXY8bVB">我打算自己回山上看看，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CpXej6rK">实在是有点放心不下山上</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jrIVjS-s">的菜地。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_0NMSArf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="b8XjjMMJ">回山。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C2TZExcr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FScsDkL6">感觉山上有点过于安静了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P7VKd0RM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yBVgFf6u">先去看菜地。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="maQpN55t">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NE6sc_F7">发现菜地还是好好的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YQLPx_tN">我这才想起，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="b2ejC9UT">山上好歹还有三师兄算是个正常人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9T9x1LQS">我真是多虑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f496qOft">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DzW5mtRm">山上一草一木照旧，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3xs_Y-vk">似乎无甚变化。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bwFTdqWq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wMKzJqZ2">直到，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cUzGfpRq">我看见了挂在师父洞府门前的</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Xyj401cQ">白底黑字挽联。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PWWK4kHK">“寿终正寝，驾鹤归西。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="25Yu7Dwp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vt7tcfjR">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5bBirpgk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ij7sg13e">咚、咚、咚——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Fca8IRad">洞府里传来了清脆的敲击声。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PF4yhNi-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2wBWVUFk">我走进洞府一看，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qJ4Te1HV">三师兄在敲木鱼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YtpCYnwe">大师兄二师兄在围观敲木鱼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
