 <p data-pid="x7dwi6B5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MhjL8DwI">“你们，在干嘛？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_Yy4wwKE">看着摆在石桌上的黄白菊花，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="d53nA4WZ">还有地上散落的黄纸钱，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aL3Vb67l">我额角青筋直跳。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JWtz2amg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D2a3FNHP">“四师弟！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-HkxstFg">那三人惊呼出声。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Fo3xmZQ2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ktRB57Av">大师兄看着我，掩面悲泣：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FFbVqkoF">“师弟，你回来得太晚了……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WDFa5g_N">师父他……走了……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xSMIarbH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rSlLQS5j">二师兄也难得的说了话：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yAzeVkWF">“师父是七日前中午走的……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WY-xaaqP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="osX3WOVb">三师兄仍闭眼敲着木鱼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-f8kI_vs">“法事是今天做的。四师弟，你正好赶上师父的头七。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MNDW9oXY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hYH_y_Kp">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EydqP7Pe">“你们为什么觉得师父死了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4WmsqSIt">我太好奇了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="w6hKPxKz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AZsZI0Wv">大师兄：“我找遍了整座山，都没看见他。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7VUyStL8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WEU9IOkM">二师兄：“五年前，师父曾说过，除非他死，否则决不下山。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r0UJPt39">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eL0jwL03">三师兄敲木鱼的手停了下来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8-77I55L">他睁开眼，说出结论：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yc_Tvd0D">“由此可知，师父，死了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Dmp4cCxI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UGnqM7zF">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-FPyF07u">逻辑鬼才了属于是。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7XeOnaas">“有没有这种可能……师父只是忘了他说过这话呢？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gOJdKUhH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KoZSjOPO">三位师兄：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6Jv_Q1ht">“……不会……吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lV7MrYX9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eQwKpdDc">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s_mPw1-K">我跟他们说，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YxJ7VfE2">师父只是下山了，还没死。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QdALX4eW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0dBUV7Fd">大师兄默默地收起了牌位，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uNy3RhnS">二师兄扫起了纸钱，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uqumZLdC">三师兄把木鱼放好。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DNo9jr9b">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3IngHF0v">“哎……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2xs16ahF">然后他们不约而同地叹了口气。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="up5Yuplu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aQ01WDPa">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Oeh4_tTZ">你们好像很失望。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Jwh8ynyq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oAR_fPgB">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ppKarCR0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mbCF-PNF">山上一切都好，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="L2N5KZ3p">我就回了医馆。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RQ6o_1Ov">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZnEDccFc">师父问我：“小四，你的师兄们怎么样？我不在山上，他们有没有偷偷说我坏话？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HDh1kuLz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Iab0_Xn4">你还挺有自知之明的嘛。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fCBEHpjB">我想了想，回答他说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o1UnO9VS">“我回去的时候，他们在哄堂大孝。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jQcDHd-5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MGvcfcGP">师父：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>9月27 再遇</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cibmcJ4i">在医馆蹭吃蹭喝了一个多月，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-l0tdAsP">终于迎来了离别。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="E0wx5Ffu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MreNSusj">师父和囡囡执手相看泪眼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bVWyyUCP">一个撅着嘴，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WTGzaBdy">一个抹着泪。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j33GKQmc">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PlNnqumT">“囡囡，阿娘走了之后，你要照顾好自己……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gHgCrkif">“呜呜呜呜阿娘放心，囡囡会乖乖的……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zUAvQWCH">“囡囡……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cBDpWl8n">“阿娘……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uQ3_up-g">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DBaHlYaX">师父蹲下，和囡囡相拥。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Uk8npJqK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aij4KCpU">我：……黄豆流汗.jpg</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UcbDaSyH">差不多得了啊，搁这演上瘾了？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I-UUqjsx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Gtfz3Mb5">老大夫：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ENNyyQcs">“囡囡，过来爷爷这里。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KolLDU74">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tki8X8ed">囡囡：“哎~”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C8vHiJpM">转身就去了老大夫身边。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XiRTS4qN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lvecOZ_a">师父：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BCduWoQ0">终究是错付了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CgO4lSg0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vUx_4qJ0">老大夫牵着囡囡小手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oiMANWpA">笑得眼角的纹路皱成鱼尾。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fq8IXobQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6aEfyNdU">门口相送。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZLhgc8Gq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qACUDxhV">老大夫拉过我，嘱咐道：“你这小兔崽子，虽然平时还挺闹腾的，但在医馆也算勤快……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XRfY4xWn">所以……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T7OjAZKy">你下次别来了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1AxlLRP4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Zl93WBpT">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2O7vha3-">你认真的？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HWGcl5kN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jdEaaSCI">老大夫看一眼又在旁边和囡囡玩耍的师父，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9Fmq3Y19">又小声补充了一句：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gMztMT6A">“起码不要带那家伙来了，太能吃了……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hiET3i-D">你自己媳妇自己养，不要啃老。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Wxum6SX1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9y6EIFmt">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DxnV5uCP">“牙齿不好，就少说点话。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iz7GvMJG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aQHTgLBU">老大夫：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eoNlKe6I">有了媳妇忘了爹。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vWyjVKTc">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Y_CN5sOM">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MegwnRqI">临末了，他站在台阶上，牵着囡囡的手，对我和师父说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wU375qb0">“近日镇里是非多，没事就待在你那破山上。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AonDyH1A">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cDXaDhl9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vtg4ogUp">回山路上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="v8rdXcVV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="X3Z93q-1">看到一佝偻着腰的乞丐拖着沉甸甸的麻袋，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NtlYkAa5">步履蹒跚，行动缓慢。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gjJddWaC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VwjDNqwu">师父突然大发善心，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kcKFozgC">停下脚步。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jLDDHBMM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l_h1y3V7">他对我说：“小四，他好可怜哦。我去看看吧！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="b3ZJ8mJI">说完就他就跑到乞丐跟前。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="c9_8f-ze">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="II93Zm8C">直觉告诉我，他要搞事情。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0Xv02Zbx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RMBg3wzW">果然，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lIMXiTW2">师父跑到人家面前，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C4ghOBT-">真的只是看看。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bj84ZMwL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Rv-3uYEl">师父：“哇，这位大哥，你这个麻袋这么大，一定很重吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uJ7S0g6v">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RADJdz_W">乞丐停下步子，用手拨开眼前的邋遢的乱发，闷声闷气地回答：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ju7OHMbS">“走开。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WJvXLvVO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jYZNSNIm">“哦。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zz8e_PHK">师父从他左边走到了右边，他又继续问：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WYUt1WFh">“这位大哥，你走这么慢，一定很累吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bBo4wDm8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5S-7ol8s">乞丐：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6xj9WBlP">“滚。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BCRpDYQL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mOY_0ocJ">“哦。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rMUYzDiN">师父原地一个空中翻滚，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8yYnmrGp">然后落在了我怀里。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JzUzcHJf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tPWGHQt-">我：淦……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xMChChKC">不得不伸手接住。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mqMiCsk9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HpNqnwKj">师父从我怀里跳下来，又跟上乞丐。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f9LDJgEO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i_PDWYSV">他伸手拦住乞丐，说道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9Cbq8t7V">“你让我走我也走了，滚也滚了……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rQ1e3twg">那么……把你的东西留下吧！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4_3HAS0C">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rmPzMdOL">师父骤然出手，从乞丐手中抢过麻袋！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cpM8WWup">乞丐身形一闪，躲了过去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gT0UxsvD">两人交起手来，你一招我一招舞得风声嚯嚯。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LolX0888">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CPN4dVhl">我：？？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cPda0vON">神展开？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z_AhHbHu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ixjKO2re">这乞丐在师父手下过了几招，竟是个高手！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6Lbsj93k">数十招后，乞丐不敌，不顾麻袋，遁走。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hiytz_RG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fWqeUd9E">他留下的麻袋静静地躺在地上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0oCuq6o4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A5i9_-4c">我看看师父，师父看看我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dttWGbRx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4uBsoaM9">我问他：“这什么？你抢人家东西干嘛？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gA00hVDE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ft8VptHK">师父摊手，无辜地眨眼：“里面的东西八成也不是他的。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n3sOGKeV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Lqt_W7Wh">“你怎么知道不是他的？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ToyKujMO">我边说边上前打开麻袋。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nM_lUTjn">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8901dQk_">师父在我身后喃喃：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eYlNdWFA">“谁会自愿被装在…………”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="szolVOzW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="E9CbKKiY">我小心翼翼地打开一点麻袋，漏出来的是上好的衣料。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wG4pqcb6">口子再开大点，我发现</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="It6o_FA6">“是人！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="X3cQmj01">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jmSPev_X">我连忙扯开整个麻袋，把昏迷的人搬出来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="81TfuKnN">看清脸，我惊呼出声：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u31Njr03">“南竹！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="njVltmRn">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1KWBCYIv">师父听见，忙凑过来看。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M0MK3wMy">“怎么是他？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x4XD2iJE">说完他急忙展开轻功就要走。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4G7_3Mob">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h8kWC56i">“你去哪？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wCKKEJEc">“追那乞丐！他怎么把人漏在这里了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ULA1og3L">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-_VWGzGr">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RMFygc--">明明你自己抢过来的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>10月2 说亲</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rQhSkvA0">我拉住了要去追人的师父。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V7ibJd2o">“别闹了，先看看南竹怎么样。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YmZeZ4Tg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8MTi6WMD">师父停下脚步，嘴巴撅得老长。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1Klg-uIj">“你骂我？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0WEDXDNA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mrrjLJI4">我：……？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RINydTur">“我没有。”</p>
 <p data-pid="T3_FlQ1i">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_ZpYS0Mf">师父：“你还不承认！你说我闹？你不知道你的一句话就可以击碎我最后的防线吗？你从不在乎我，你只关心他！你从来不在乎我的伤心绝望，却对他嘘寒问暖！小四！你给我等着，我要让你知道骂我的下场！我要你一辈子活在愧疚之中！我走了，你可不要追我！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KDcnlC-V">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FISGlMP2">他作势要走。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WoFwYcyl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oT2TdTGe">我没有阻拦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="13B2Ws81">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CbhgPBXB">一刻钟后，师父站在两尺之外，是的，一刻钟他只挪动了两尺。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4Bwc5NYr">他回头，跺脚。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1ETwvYez">“你果然不在乎我！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LnWEVVB0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XPe_WMpg">我：“玩够了就帮我把南竹抬到医馆去。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="57gF6dXs">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="20nsm0-M">师父：……</p>
 <p data-pid="YxMnCl7P"><br>
  “哦。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="URlAWgRO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kULie0ZT">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bHXkSCoc">医馆，敲门。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5YpIe0m9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UunKmKPc">“谁啊？今日闭馆……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KLmrEsWT">老大夫的声音由远及近，他开了条门缝，瞥见是我，啪一声，门合上了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WhFoYLvH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rSOS6xk8">可恶！这老头子竟然真的不想见我！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KdLD1Mvr">——</p>
 <p data-pid="Mklums4B">老头还是开门了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZgCeimVW">据说是因为囡囡听见我的声音，吵着要见我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="197MhxSO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wwE67y4v">师父把南竹放到医馆地上，对老大夫说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r-vJNeUI">“岳父，看看这小子怎么样，还能活多久？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="c8ann_Y-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qEGctEmD">老大夫检查了一番昏迷的南竹，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PR6a1rR3">摇摇头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1viaYHZr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TdbOajWK">师父：“活不成了？正好，长剑山后山腰上有块地……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pwNLgQ_O">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2NACLv5p">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OJy5Yfky">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5SK5Iz79">老大夫：“噢，不。我是说他没事。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NmQDNWMk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1Jn_UOd7">“那他怎么昏迷不醒？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uTh5_kR2">“你们有没有想过……可能，他只是睡着了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1mzJCSoO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uPUERYPF">我：？？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WtK4TDvI">真的吗？又不是猪，怎么会被人装进麻袋这么折腾都不醒！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Y3j40cj-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RM2s6GI6">老大夫眯起眼：“你在质疑我的医术？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="75Q3IinY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vcNbvgYU">不敢。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="X1CZ5N3r">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5gBW0plr">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ki05bjCm">南竹醒了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7oTFGbvT">他未睁开眼，尚在迷茫中，口中含糊唤道：“……时辰……到了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zaKy84Ga">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JpVrbSYg">没人应南竹，他似乎感到哪里不对了，睁开眼。只见，我、师父、老大夫、囡囡，站在床边围成圈看他。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Af6Win9D">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Bm9-DtHb">南竹：啊！！！！！！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sWShR1Wu">救命！怎么回事？他们怎么在这？不对，他怎么在这？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IFlIKTKv">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wVyy3hi7">老大夫看一眼我，得意地摸了摸胡子：“我就说，他是睡着了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9-uSTf2_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gWi97jJA">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jhyO10z1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ebEoeYEu">听我说完状况，南竹似乎没有意识到自己差一点被绑走了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dmNxLf0J">他表情愣愣的，许久才憋出一句话。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LGvwYFFp">“真的吗？不会是你打算把我掳上山当压寨夫人吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="noB_4KtX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hC5hDj5E">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H6LAQo8p">抽刀。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vrt1c9LD">“再说话就把你埋长剑山上。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WR9rvx-T">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xf8DvuMa">南竹笑嘻嘻地跳下床，手臂搭上我的肩膀，说道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZH29PE7U">“开玩笑的。朱珏，这次多谢你了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WjLFxY0u">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wyrmzDVT">师父：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FE5wH9Xx">他出现在南竹身后，阴恻恻地问道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bdPpUWR_">“小五，好久不见啊……怎么也不跟师父问声好？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="b1xBPukf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N_A67a0_">“师……师……师父！您也在啊？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aMsS-kLA">南竹咻一声躲到我身后。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i_DQoyBW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6dby6iqK">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hwH2Ga93">敢情我说了这么多，你完全没注意到师父也在？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J-mCLoZB">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6JW737uC">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lrDMYTEx">没啥大事，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u5BIB6M9">我准备和师父回山了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J8xVZKkf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p-gq5bJf">南竹抱着我的腿，哭道：“朱珏，你别走！我害怕！万一那歹徒又回来找我怎么办？我这么一个文质彬彬的公子哥怎么打得过他啊……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZYS811eJ">你带我回长剑山如何？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UpTGliku">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YhFFzcuI">我无情抽腿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NkBCoIRy">“让南府给你请个护卫。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R6eWXOx8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DPNBQnUf">师父点头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6m0rPWSi">“就是就是。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KRby4iMI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rGPgAUbM">“我不能回府！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Pp2XUVLE">南竹一狠心，摊牌了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="X_DwZWOw">“不能回去！最近我爹说要给我找个媳妇，过几日就要押着我成亲了！我不想成亲，其实……那乞丐是我雇来助我出府的！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mQRpWhxi">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lbP7Nbyk">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8Pl6rlJS">啊这……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QuuEnR6X">离大谱。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>10月4 两幅面孔</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="56Lnom4W">南竹抱着我的腿哭诉：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g3P-XVJM">“事情是这样的，我爹说我年纪不小了。人又好吃懒做，该找个媳妇来管管我……叽里呱啦叽里咕噜……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NEG3uoLV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5fVHOB-O">总之就是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tBsmXYF6">他想逃婚，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zCR3iOL5">于是买通了府里倒垃圾的大叔，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lSMOQVGE">偷偷把自己带出来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DOdtPX8x">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s4cySy_n">等等，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wB2ADP_V">那之前装南竹的麻袋……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N412AAhq">是垃圾袋！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gvCDQBeF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3BmpdMax">我往后一跳，远离了南竹。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pvvnaT5F">怪不得他身上好像有股味。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2wRPWuY1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HqTIE-9i">我看一眼那麻袋，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xHm7Rz4Y">对南竹说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SuzOw5yy">“你也算找准了自己的定位。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wa4RR8K0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9Je8e0U2">南竹：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-Nsq0cWW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9mdRsCED">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a2e5XIWm">故事听完了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7p_DD-iN">我掏掏耳朵迈腿就走，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R7wZWjkZ">准备回山。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YHsAlLHw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0eEm9ugo">南竹又扑了上来：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BYSKvfHL">“你不带我走吗？我爹现在说不定在满城找我，你不帮我，我一定会被抓回去的……呜呜呜呜……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vL3ZHLM_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RQqRCoTS">我：“不帮。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0eWf3ty1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QQ3MfsmD">略略略略</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bBC1x8B6">师父得意地对南竹扮鬼脸。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AOhTFUJ6">哼，凭你也配踏入我长剑山。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A-7q6S0A">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uLeDIawU">南竹从怀里摸出了一把银票。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OIul1sUT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3r6ZLNck">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jCIGc86Q">“不帮……是不可能的。你我认识这么多年，我不能坐视不管！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EAbm5ABZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rUYxE_Ua">师父：……？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VjSuissD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GE5lFsAZ">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GNgcq35Z">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LNfOy2EP">再次和老大夫道别。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IcTLwYyF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="38D18YlX">老大夫：“滚吧。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nX8cf3gO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GVJyypl8">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FYpJAMT4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2atusxnk">真回山里了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="98jarGN4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dKrbCx6p">见到我们回来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="X_AXNmLm">大师兄二师兄三师兄很高兴，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BPovcscA">一个个面带喜色地冲过来</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M38eCHH0">迎接南竹。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9_5PbokM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kHtvt6fU">我和师父被挤到了一边。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4YKh7wdU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0ShqCF2A">只听见那几人簇拥着南竹，鞍前马后道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="18uCyV8J">“许久不见，五师弟越发英俊了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FqE0uJ_P">“谢宵说得对。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DrzPyfLS">“师弟此番住多久？是不走了吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RH1ZWQtv">“老三此言有理，依我看五师弟和长剑山有缘，不如长住……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oxFYL56u">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PxZoJUh-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Hyb3buCb">南竹几乎是被师兄们架着胳膊走的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BwDbF4Sd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O2x5bLa7">看着他们走远的背影，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YeaYOeYT">我问师父：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Yc7-q3L4">“师父，师兄们很喜欢南竹？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GYxIcSis">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NRpDlRQL">师父冷笑一声：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6Yhk3v2z">“就他们那德性，百里之外都能嗅着铜臭味。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i1ejb1wx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6I7XRBe7">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="46-JHZ7I">总感觉自己也被内涵了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iW7BljVx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OXRbTP5Z">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ph17R2AF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jT412QpF">回山的第二天，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qu2IYSnt">师父闭关了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eawEVi81">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bQaiwj0J">我望望天，打个哈欠。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wlTahPno">朴实无华的山顶洞人生活又开始了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wKaZTVzR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T4C2ZgIV">我发现南竹挑剔得很。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k1ocVoOE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GpcB892c">早上送粥，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i1jwUYj9">他说是糙米吃不下。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="E2fei5Fx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LCLXB1ut">我忍。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N0ufU88H">买了精米回来熬粥。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EpSrUmFr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4245vn22">中午吃饭，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zke5gAuf">他说菜太少没胃口。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DSFeeNKm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9F3147uq">我再忍。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-wZ_Z8_4">又做了三个菜。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2JrftY0P">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tPa-M7O6">晚上睡觉，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MX_Ay2bI">他说石床太硬难入眠。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cpWh5CsI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UhDd-L52">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7ZqERVPE">在沉默中握紧了刀。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="doXcBt3w">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="d3qxMcxx">南竹拿起白花花的银票扇风，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nJuCxRW9">“这天儿可真热。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9VRf-VBA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="loCWbuEB">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SV4Uj4Ap">放下了刀，并且给他添了两床褥子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D1kBG8i0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vMMg5paW">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_LsBtNq6">七天后，遭不住了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SDvRH8O3">这人睡觉要人扇风、穿衣服要人伺候、喝水要帮吹凉的……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Od0k_dzt">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="914UT3dG">我悄悄问几位师兄：“上次南竹在山上也这么能折腾？你们咋忍的？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XDkGi-42">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Z8SFeR5K">大师兄：哈？折腾？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="auex1x-7">“五师弟不是乖得很吗？上次还特意端了两盘菜孝敬我。还送了白玉扇……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KsvouTxm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aK3LPOMV">二师兄点点头：“他送了我一套城中锦绣坊新出的留仙裙。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2bOmXbRC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="biit7P9g">三师兄：“五师弟送了小僧一串小叶紫檀佛珠。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G1OOA3_L">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VKMtsRGn">我：？？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Or2VWeW4">这小东西还有两幅面孔？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1WmE4SiU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-UyhUn9K">大师兄突然拿起扇子一敲三师兄的脑壳，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C5a8o51E">笑道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p9I32RLh">“老三啊老三，你不是答应了五师弟别说的吗？出家人可不能打诳语。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oLE5TGq3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Vpuu9BjG">三师兄吃痛，回怼：“你不也说了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rpEq0kLR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-Uage-rQ">？？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BkjGbZ-1">爷笑了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DMgz4Gjw">所以你们一个个都瞒着我？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QL4Sz7qk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KL0lxqYh">别跑！看刀！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l_rCQzRy">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fKvFMVAK">“四师弟，我不是有意的！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kV3XlH2G">“他给的实在太多了！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IFmE7iVz">“所以留仙裙又有什么错？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="InCxt4yX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yBs9umZT">追不上师兄们，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gYxPFrWe">我怒气冲冲地提刀杀到南竹洞府。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ephJ4HTz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="F6_kLMFk">南竹正嗑着瓜子看话本，见我来，说道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BIxBq6PY">“你来得正好，这本快看完了，你明日下山帮我买最新的一册。别的不要，只要翠竹阁的，纸张好些。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vqU3Ds0Y">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8oIN8iKR">我笑了笑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0KMGZByd">“好，明天就烧给你。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>10月12 反客为主</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9zCCiRoZ">啊啊啊啊啊啊</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PxHXaDQs">啊啊啊啊啊啊——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VxDj7P7N">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4RA4DuIx">凄厉的惨叫声绵延不绝，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wVWYf95w">长剑山上的鸟雀骇起腾飞。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qxthIFV9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DPhNd9El">南竹面上青一块紫一块的，瑟瑟发抖地躲在石桌下。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0gy8KjN5">“朱珏，不要打了不要打了！我错了！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QmmLsxuu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KYHQVknV">“哦？错哪了？你说来听听？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C9KDZVON">我捏捏拳头，一脚踏在石凳上，居高临下地俯视他。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0C1DJo8O">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H2mqbpKd">“我......不该和师兄们私相授受......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O3-rQfZC">“你心里门儿清呐？平时使唤我使唤得这么起劲，到师兄们面前就这么能奉承？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="c6elJYEZ">“这不......我们相识这么多年，我还没见过你服侍人的样子......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zJyRbGv4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qO1t2j2C">“哟，那南大公子还满意我的服务吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1nli1Vk_">我伸出铁手，温柔地拽起南竹的衣领。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a_SVbmkh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u2ahlJyW">南竹咽了咽口水，唯唯诺诺道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gHnFzIvS">“满意......QAQ”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6C0Ot2A6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HmjcoKar">这正是我想听到的，我捏他衣领的手略微收紧，笑问：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0oV4OQHE">“南大公子既然满意小人的服务，那这赏钱给是不给.....”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Fdnf_lrL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OCEXOYgp">“给......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Nd_WF3GG">许是被吓怕了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u-825Cam">南竹很干脆地掏出了一沓银票放到我手上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A4351LE7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0Xa5FZpv">算你识相！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="epwit99y">我接过银票，打算清点一下。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ptkACIMV">然后我的笑容绷住了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="L1zTOlwm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K2Hau7MP">这一沓钱......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Vj2CAofq">只有夹在最边上的那两张是票子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="napjEfpZ">中间竟全是白纸！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kWhtHucH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pu8JMDFr">南竹见我瞪他，心虚地移开视线。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JQfmi0TZ">“钱都用来孝敬师兄们了......只剩这么两张......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kxu5k0qO">——</p>
 <p data-pid="Z_F03eTE">我：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tkos7qzZ">震怒！︵╰（‵□′）╯︵</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jrBR_sNk">既然没钱，那就不要怪我心狠手辣！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WhnzMW8b">我露出了一个丧心病狂的笑容。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MLlbuwWu">——</p>
 <p data-pid="-3qrtFOU">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VsYTN2jY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D1WErqP3">盛怒之下，我决定惩罚南竹。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qbgPL-ta">天天使唤我，还只给这么点工资？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W34sZEDV">我这个人向来睚眦必报，谁让我不爽了，我必定加倍奉还！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rMeauFE1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MNi2Wg7X">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mMRIGCxn">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="slcSmIKo">把笤帚塞到南竹手中，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8RIb8cJI">我说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ay0TmlWo">“今天不扫完洞府不许休息。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qxmnFNa9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YFPmkku2">南竹：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wrQp-fr0">“行吧。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uz2DbEqr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LA8Mayxc">只是我忽略了一点，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fRJ-2qjV">他从未做过粗重活，笨手笨脚的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i2cpyF-U">一会儿撞倒了木凳，一会儿碰碎了茶杯，一会儿又摔裂了铜镜......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2AYizaDS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="w6Jt8LGz">我：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rAwVdN9p">心在滴血。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q7EjTn6_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="13cekUg6">决定换个方式罚他。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lFRKSfHQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qoheIBa5">于是，我对南竹说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HgfWHBim">“去打盘水来。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_xTXaeEJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="w8Zw87vw">南竹：“哦。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NNCt0GMk">他应声，顺从地出门打水。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fdqNOGJk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dwH7UsGZ">我：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aYD73qzb">不妙的预感。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="No5fpAmI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="usZXrF8h">碰——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="v29RhTR-">门外传来一声巨响，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0wHY0HLm">水盆打翻了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VBZyz8MD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Xfpgkpnx">我：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fzz1Xhym">可恶，早该知道会这样。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3KE9lBVj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fTeSPas3">亲自去打了盆水，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1urQPHIU">放到石床前的地上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jVRvKLpL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jQW7CnZm">坐在床边，我望着南竹，伸出了jio。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nzJJNL04">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-Ho0JBNA">南竹：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hO3Z01FM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OSzL1bCA">我挑衅地晃了一下jio，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GWDAIdiR">冷酷无情地开口：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PoKOKKc5">“愣着干嘛？给我洗脚。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LoFpdQwh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AdJ69vhj">南竹：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r9k-guXe">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D-ALTsSo">见人不动，我皱起了眉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LB2FVevr">让他给我洗脚......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f8bmWRyO">好像有点太折辱人了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XZEeJo_N">要不换一个......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5KK59p0g">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K3YXQBTZ">我正打算改口，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O51bHPK0">却听见南竹说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="offjiPKD">“这个盆......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WRHERqcz">是你的洗脸盆。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Khukr-qs">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4ptsyXMU">我：......？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j_lxhyCH">咳咳</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qto_W4yp">不好意思，拿错了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rmUhuOAy">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uiPzS2sO">南竹叹了一口气，走出洞府。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9WlYAghT">半晌，他端着脚盆进来了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="INykmoJ0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="etBlU-o5">难得，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N30-UCKa">这次倒没有打翻。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AtHgtRtZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oI_XC5x7">他在床前放下水盆，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iXTncYkW">然后蹲下握住了我的小腿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1NnkkMwN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cmk4axNT">我一惊，差点踹一脚他。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wssnEbHf">“你干嘛？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fpHxG9Gh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DVx1wX2o">南竹抬头：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Wt7aJvgx">“洗脚啊。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cKzPnkzE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SGPIh-tC">我：......</p>
 <p data-pid="TnWeELpO">哦。</p>
 <p data-pid="VP2XeovY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FJOUju7_">他脱了我的鞋袜，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YjVO1DBi">慢慢把我的双脚浸在水中。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u5tOaW9V">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VQgsthtr">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UNKkhg9P">水是温热的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j43T6r22">算他会做。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8GzRuZ71">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NUaM_2ov">泡了一会儿，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-kCOauHN">我寻思也差不多了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IPbGXho4">让养尊处优富家公子给我端水洗jio，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lEe2JVEf">够打击人了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="apH8XvvK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XmPSiyaU">“咳......得，你可以......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8pEHEal_">正想让南竹走，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eILgYfA2">他却突然伸手握住了我的脚踝。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Bqwr_XTf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W_D1jeGg">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tgswB_gu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GQcs7dTI">他低头看着水盆，沉默了一会儿，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0IKJ_qXE">才缓缓开口道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TJ5BflBj">“要不要......按跷？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j_oyulJr">我听闻......按揉足下的几个穴位可舒缓疲劳。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>10月17 洗脚</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LEHq6JZx">嗯？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="enjZkVZ5">我挑起眉，将信将疑地点了点头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="937Yz7g1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9lCs8VpR">南竹向脚盆伸出了手。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EpWgWPoN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wlKV06fS">一刻钟后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J1H8tcYL">哈哈哈哈哈哈哈哈哈</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gxXWutV-">哈哈哈哈哈哈哈好痒</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uvi_6PDu">救命哈哈哈哈哈哈哈</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bocIRCa0">我笑得方圆十里鸟兽惊散长剑山地崩山摧壮士死然后天梯石栈相钩连。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kA4-nHa1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3TiAq_uo">南竹脸上全是水珠。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HmEgs6uW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3raUcYXD">呃，是我乱踢脚溅上去的水。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="S-1duzfQ">怪不好意思的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CL8TLKJr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5p7XEcqP">南竹一脸无语，左手还抓着我的一只脚，便用右手抹了一下面上的水。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="c--MucS9">他说：“有这么好笑吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kyIrsidh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xC5nepRY">我惊恐地瞪大了双眼(⊙o⊙)</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="otr_JQK8">“你的手刚摸过我脚，还擦脸！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sLi0udYz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jii9Ub8R">南竹：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P-liomDt">草......草率了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vlduxVFx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nWimfSqo">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Huegi-6Q">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qhlXaBOt">洗脚一事后，我算是原谅南竹这孙子了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5v-FkJaK">不过南竹好像转性了，对于此事耿耿在怀，说什么不能白白让我伺候他这么久，他要补偿我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6p-LciJe">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ybyDLzf_">看着他真诚的眼神，我也不好拒绝。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l2j57QZ8">反正洞府里值钱的东西都已经被摔碎，没什么可以再摔了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lPszCmJb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mh0ZLKO8">于是，南大公子开始了他的男仆体验生涯。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-hJXILCK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZnEiY9yK">早起，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DTHDJpt6">南竹说要帮我穿衣。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YcsLmU8m">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gFylMY72">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Qq4Pgxyl">可以，但没有必要。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tski4D3g">我古怪地看他一眼，拿过衣服自己穿了起来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7BlSb122">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t7Yxacuf">晚上睡觉，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GH9BCesp">南竹说要帮我暖被子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W15bLMXp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tvOSpmmD">我：？？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-IKVzhSJ">“从我的床上滚下来。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bz6PQ4kF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BKeR5kwL">南竹抬起手臂闻一闻衣袖，说道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ARHolNdh">“放心，我沐浴了，身上没味道。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="51ezvjaP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BnOtxF0f">我：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qA9DUEr7">“现在tm是夏天你暖个*床。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vvvxQ-NZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cI7Wc-wf">“快起开，我要睡觉。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="js_0JeAP">“哦......那你睡前要按跷吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BqdJDqKE">“不了，再笑一回我怕长剑山受不住要裂开。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ut1XIq_f">“哦......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q1WYg5Ld">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3m3DwjOz">南竹离开了我的洞府，不知道为啥总觉得他的背影带着些许遗憾（？）</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Mpw_4W_X">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="od_sdXHS">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wIKj9-Ec">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lSgvKxd5">第二天，早起。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rMM8JvR4">南竹捧着脸帕出现，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="komp21We">“要洗漱吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tW7cTb7y">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NjPQi_5Z">我：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MKKbT3F0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vo8Wk5Qc">洗澡，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="twqZITXu">南竹在屏风外喊：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="271aPO9g">“要加水吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MwnXsEqd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PHe7dDQ_">我：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HFLASKA3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3N6YkEkc">三天，只用了三天。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pq8Ex1ak">我求着南竹不要再伺候我了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MNLug-BE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Pntw9of9">南竹挠头：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2V5x8zwO">“为何？说出来你可能不信，我觉得自己还挺有干这行的天赋的。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m7nK5aSL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2T_E_9My">我：“憋说了，算我怕你，你收拾收拾下山吧。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KMECxk67">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NpJSj9LV">南竹秒变脸，声泪俱下：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YqTyTj_3">“呜呜呜呜呜呜呜呜呜......你个没良心的要赶我走！当初有银票的时候叫我小甜甜如今我身无分文就赶我走......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fVipfDrg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lbLqIZ6g">我：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cyrRpap6">住嘴，我没叫过你小甜甜。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>10月24 买米</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ezkSvtt7">南竹死死地抱住我的腿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LjgxPuQY">“我不走！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qb9Z9irb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8gCjzNA9">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tfwoqv_7">“不走就不走，放开我的腿。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xTByCQ64">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T12SRQI4">南竹抱得更紧了：“我不！你肯定是想趁我不备扔我下山！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XYHikfEN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-5GqTxyz">我：呵呵</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O1Wg4N9L">“你不放手，我也可以把尸体扔下山。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Y01veWir">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VPJi8lhq">南竹弱弱松开了手。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rnJeQRpL">真是的，非要我吓唬人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nJTp1EHN">我摇摇头，说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hZfa70FM">“你下山……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-DXN5T4A">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H04hG9GU">南竹：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Uz-bd2MF">“大骗子！又赶我走……呜呜呜呜┮﹏┮”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ayO6FaLk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2CiXw_1V">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4QMx28ce">“住嘴，你跟我下山买点粮食和家用。知道你这几天摔了多少东西吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Gna282q0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bTxv5Bfk">南竹：(⊙x⊙)</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UFgo8yno">“哦。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jc_RZUUy">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RrFihUQB">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="41C4_jXR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5rRVS6IF">下山。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="e1Mepd9z">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4YRNjzDG">粮食铺籴米。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BW689thh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q8yBmkWa">买了足足两石米。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PtDfc55P">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fZVBcFlg">掌柜震惊，看看我，又看看南竹：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yCMnbsWL">“二位可需小店差人将米送到府上？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QaCpgLRS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NNpUO3Zi">我摇头：“不用，我二人即可。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fW6hnfan">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x0iXGuxo">掌柜再震惊，打量一下南竹，然后一脸痛惜地对我说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LcEcT0jk">“大丈夫竟吝啬至此！你夫人这样文静瘦弱，怎可做粗重活？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gsNWSH8p">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jFgWBouq">南竹隔着面纱捂住嘴：憋笑.jpg</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-lX6AQTl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Kys_7Pxl">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FVJJ4hl3">顿时明白了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sF8adkY5">下山时，南竹说怕撞见南府的人，于是借了二师兄的衣裙穿还戴了面纱……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bvGLfyKZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="F_VCIPTk">掌柜看我的眼神好像在看渣男。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Dp7Bfxhe">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oMAcrLZs">南竹趁机挽我的手臂，捏着嗓子矫揉造作道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SNzp-2_r">“掌柜的不必为妾担忧，家中贫寒，夫君也是无可奈何。妾已经习惯了………”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MlrniYzW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9stFk3cv">感觉掌柜要呸我一口了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yE7GCsK3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u2J8ckt2">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K6dSh2A5">南竹这个臭猪！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tj1JJk8w">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="27hzO15e">我勾唇一笑，扒拉南竹的手臂，颐指气使道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wANo25Oi">“不是习惯了吗？愣着干嘛，还不快去搬米。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OkgpKLrH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u4jfoUbz">掌柜：呸。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KlFCCrmH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ybvtgVoW">我对他说：“不会吧不会吧？不会没见过吃软饭的吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1ImWNbyM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xzfEbNu9">掌柜：厚颜无耻之徒！呸！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h0p3vjWY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lsF5f8ik">那一天后，城中开始流传一位软饭男的故事。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="64B1bduY">他相貌俊美却厚颜无耻，偏生娶的夫人温柔可人又力大无穷能单肩抗两石米……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JPCsBsoi">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ECDRT-S8">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xp_j-f-U">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qJkKD9c6">事实上呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OiL0LGKK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="b84kyxf8">回山的路上，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nlDiyrVK">我一个人扛着两袋米。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R-IrJlAh">南竹在旁边喊加油。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oU2R9DBW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ke_R_-Rm">我：I'm fine.</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="64yt4Ivh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sNMmPsx2">南竹：“朱珏，你累不累，要不要歇歇？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CUFC3qVp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hFEdCbXS">我：“你要是闭嘴我就能没这么累了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mExauX7C">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0y83b4WN">南竹突然又捏起嗓子：“夫君~你看看你，都热出汗了,妾帮你擦擦~”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p3hiIaKJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qOv8xemC">我：yue</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JERMtDKT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="30U3dY4e">南竹：哈哈哈哈哈哈哈</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TwAeyDFK">“我学得像不像？我爹纳的那几个妾就总这样跟他说话。你说好不好笑？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A19YmLbd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cu0ycrQ0">我没有笑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_CiV2LhK">但他几乎笑出眼泪。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HPtp4QEq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WoschDK6">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oChFKM8Q">“不想笑就别笑，难看。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T-Cl1q7M">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Fdjuc1Ic">南竹收了声音，沉默一阵。又忽然小跑跟上来，从我肩上卸下一袋米放到自己肩上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PlPD2i55">“还挺沉。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6QBP4eyG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dzTSfD0m">“朱珏，你买的这些米够山上吃多久？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DL5R9kvy">“很快。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R_ZedoYK">“为何？好像挺多的。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7NXQegby">“因为猪要出圈了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9sEqsHkx">“？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jGAYJWWE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>10月30 门派恋情</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Fo7nV4fQ">师父即将出关。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8bN3HvYZ">我和南竹站在岩洞外恭候。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XaaVe1RH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kxo8aM1g">为啥只有我俩？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N2aUubcv">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i94w1UX5">大师兄跟二师兄闹别扭了，没来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="L1RVr4Ez">三师兄说师父出关多大点事儿，有迎接他的功夫不如下山化个缘，也没来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="acIoKyRj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="khIoZGcm">望了下日影，我估摸着时辰将至。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WGNbZOkd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="c2GLCxj4">果然，下一刻</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uO7XyFuK">一颗白色炮弹从岩洞里飞了出来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aKjJIQJ9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H3x2mI6P">师父从洞府飞奔而出，像个树袋熊一样挂在我身上，头埋在我颈窝里磨蹭，嚷嚷道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZaUSsjHT">“呜呜呜呜终于出关了！我好想好想小四啊，小四有没有好想好想师父？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4q9iUnnP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PjSaNCgM">我：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ry30aFth">“好......好......重......快滚下来。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5MR42dhw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CrMK1KTD">师父：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7J6xaOWK">你不宠我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZyUqBy52">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sUJiHrXY">然后他一转头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ktGXMWvT">看见南竹也在，顿时垮起脸。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ut3l8_TJ">“你咋也在？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZqXPDpC9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k5vd-0l1">南竹：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4PWH7pIH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0OLXepOC">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nCYjoPM9">师父一出关就嚷嚷着饿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Bht-wDLz">我做了饭，看着他吃。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aOA52j1f">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rwZ93XWX">越看越感觉哪里怪怪的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="arnqZHPY">他好像比以前高了，脸颊的肉肉少了，头发也更卷了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dnJbNcz_">最重要的是......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_2B0Xjo4">更能吃了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="d6SUoX5h">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o8fAkb8z">舀了第五碗米饭给他。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wwpPhDoK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="w2zw-Pn1">我冲南竹使了个眼色：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dE3_9XMQ">猪，出圈，懂？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W6K_wSms">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ql3r4kiY">南竹：恍然大悟.jpg</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3Pvo2ak1">懂了懂了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SQO__G3w">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uOUtLNP0">不知咋滴，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_lPXdKI0">埋头干饭的师父放下筷子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2g_qlabG">转头问我：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xVWLnpus">“小四，你和小五眉来眼去干什么？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_OjOnPBt">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PmHQvatq">我：……？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Is5IW9Fp">“啊？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LvrE4Xka">这你也能看见？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="w1IRPqHa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="c_K4GD1z">不待我回应，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3U73IFTl">师父又看向南竹，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J40Yai_U">超凶的。\(｀ ○′)/</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NMqzOoAa">“小五，我跟你说，我们长剑山有门规，不可以搞门派恋情的！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tfhgRDm_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P1mbyRuk">南竹：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yOSnya3a">“可是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0TuJocuG">你已经将我逐出长剑派了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zaTv9gUZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ccUrcfCM">师父：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iYM337_N">忘记了……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YSE9Wkl8">“那我再收你做徒弟吧……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xDyZ45sq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AMFIKxJr">南竹：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DS5m21Be">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u4mLnyNa">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O8rkXYXp">“不是，长剑派什么时候有门规这么正式的东西了？我咋不知道？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uuh2zd_6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ajqEgjY5">师父很理直气壮：“我方才定的！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x83M7GeK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l5ybkRZu">我不禁皱起了眉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6g2t-kiL">“这样吗？可是我看到大师兄和二师兄亲嘴了……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wD2cOY6-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1UKEu_gQ">师父：！？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vkBALLIX">南竹：！？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l45TPmP8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LZsRYJCt">“竟有这事？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7mM2MBHN">“说来听听？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CSdPtE1e">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XTRXRgPo">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="80wY2A7o">离我远点，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sgMQYyBE">耳朵贴太近了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hsqFBQSW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N5a3r1ak">我开始讲述那天看到的事情。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cnbJWYkO">吧啦吧啦吧啦</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Iaa3hAv8">吧啦吧啦吧啦</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h8DPZ4dF">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="He_-IZlZ">“……就是这样，我听见二师兄洞府里传来打斗声，急忙前去。甫一开门，只见二师兄躺在地上，大师兄趴在二师兄身上，两人嘴对嘴……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O8--k1Pr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o1Ccl7QH">师父单手支着下巴，皱眉思索：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1ax8cUUD">“老大老二这么野的吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h5oc2dbF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s3ECCaKC">南竹羞涩道：“然后呢？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NyFSQ_6C">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jHiesfkL">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0jzy4i2f">你不对劲。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XfrMmvW4">“自然是没有然后了，我赶紧跑了。怕被杀人灭口。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vEL76Zp7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uRy1smQb">师父闻言，拍拍我的肩膀，坚定地说：“小四你放心，有我在，老大老二动不了你。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W3yd93z4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kcKpwy8x">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-AHEvveB">谢谢。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qQkPOTW-">那只是夸张的说法啦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>11月6 醉后胡言</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7l_uwkfg">后来我仔细斟酌了一下，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MV_OVCLh">有点担心师父会反对大师兄和二师兄在一起。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TLtRSbgU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2cYsXdq7">趁着师父还在吃饭，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lH-zgNVR">我决定去通风报信。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YTtPkVeT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BLx1J73n">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wyiQ4OvL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lASDv5_n">“大师兄！大事不好了！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TAexDnbd">我气喘吁吁地跑去找大师兄。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PH3EaEBo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FB-sigF8">一进屋里，酒气熏天，我差点闻yue了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cdDWG0nA">只见大师兄正抱着酒罐子，披头散发面色愁苦，一口一口地闷酒。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7shYvPQF">听见我唤，他摇摇晃晃地站起，问道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9NN4BaN7">“是……四师弟呀。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eTjc94zn">什么事？师父被妖怪抓走了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zffdjPhF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zOGlcXZ5">我有点急。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Db_gEIoU">“比这个严重！他可能要来抓你和二师兄！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BXv8wvMi">你们快私奔吧！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T6liwhd8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rOHuoWNx">大师兄脑袋一歪，只捕捉到关键词：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hbVievVb">“二师兄？孟岚，他怎么了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IKgxVD6u">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D9Gk6yXI">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oPlU8a-k">他醉得厉害，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vDt_WIMl">我也不多说，直接去拉了二师兄来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P8jMOw8d">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0um1yv1s">二师兄正在给留仙裙熏香，被我强行拽了来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yyWhp21l">他见大师兄喝得稀醉，啧一声就嫌弃地别开眼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tG5vxgAW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8lPYemve">二师兄礼貌地笑着:）对我说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9MLh5cMS">“老四，你最好找我真的有事。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Mw3Jox-K">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l-9BtQkN">我戳了戳手指，小声说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nHGTvnCc">“也不算什么大事……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h52OllAp">就是……师父知道你和大师兄在一起了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HGD9fZBg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rXl7W_49">我越说越小声。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IjkgtO0X">好心虚呀。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3qrNjXmk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zXhJuOen">大师兄显然没听懂我在说啥，只一个劲儿往二师兄身边凑，被推开了又往前凑，还委屈巴巴地哭。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GDdah2GY">“孟岚……哇哇哇哇o(╥﹏╥)o……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0wlnoq0p">孟岚你为什么不理我？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q4V61zPb">哇哇哇……孟岚你怎么不说话</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U1IJo-sf">孟岚你说句话啊……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Zlh6k-jo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yoUfIsK0">二师兄脸色微妙，一手推开蹭鼻子上脸的大师兄，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SuAhJXuK">扭头对我说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q5ZPME3X">“你说什么？谁和谢宵在一起了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2e186s3N">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dfSI04tJ">我：“别瞒了，上回你俩亲嘴，我看见了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0pFBwCwS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="830tGWWk">二师兄的脸瞬间涨红。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_QIgeZ7p">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Rpx4-FWL">“闭嘴！那是意外！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3FWV_mp2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DUBb5PVk">我：“真的吗？我不信。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MT3-_vJU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j_88n_hq">师父点头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KlWiSgQv">“我也不信。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KUwI1m10">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SXlF6TWo">嗯？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IT-b3mwU">师父？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1d_maa-S">！！！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2ED0X5_g">“师父你怎么来了？！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rCeGg4c9">我连忙抱住师父，大吼：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PdE5Yh8m">“二师兄你快带大师兄跑，这里有我拖着他！</p>
